○ Ministry of Interior Requests Interpretation of the Administrative Appeal Law: The Ministry of Interior yesterday submitted a report to the Executive Yuan stating that Article 1 of the Administrative Appeal Law stipulates that people may file an administrative appeal if their rights or interests are harmed due to illegal or improper actions by central or local government agencies. However, the text only mentions "people" and does not mention "officials." If an official is subject to administrative punishment, can they file an administrative appeal as a "person"? It seems necessary to have an interpretation. As this concerns legal interpretation, the Ministry is not in a position to make a decision and therefore submits the Administrative Appeal Law for referral to the Judicial Yuan for interpretation.

○ Hunan Province's Regional Bandit Suppression Plan

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province has suffered greatly from the Communist scourge for the past three years and has not had a single day of peace. During the war against the Gui army, the Communist bandits took the opportunity to stir up trouble. Peng Dehuai disrupted Pingyue, Huang Gonglue and Kong Hezhong disrupted Liuyang and Liling, He Long disrupted Nanhua, and Zhou Wen disrupted Yangming. In addition, bandits have sprung up like bees in the Xiangxi region's Chenyuan area and the Xiangzhong region's Baowu area. Travelers are wary on the roads. Almost none of the province's 76 counties are clean. However, the bandit scourge varies in size. He Jian has decided to take advantage of the end of the campaign against the Gui army to launch a large-scale suppression campaign, dividing the province into five bandit suppression zones and assigning forces of four divisions and one garrison command to be responsible for each zone, starting on August 1st and aiming to eliminate all bandits in each zone within two months. The allocated regional plan was officially announced yesterday with the following order: "Investigating that this time, the Gui rebels have roamed through various places in Hunan Province, looting and leaving behind firearms, and the Communist bandits have taken the opportunity to be rampant, endangering public security, it is necessary to divide the regions to search and thoroughly eliminate them. We must eradicate the roots to ensure local stability. The following regulations are hereby stipulated for the bandit suppression zones of each unit: (1) Changsha, Yueyang, Linxiang, Ningxiang, Xiangyin, Pingjiang, Liuyang, and Liling counties are the bandit suppression zone of the 15th Division, with Division Commander Wei Suzhong as the commander. (2) Hengyang, Hengshan, Qiyang, Lingling, Dong'an, Leiyang, Yongxing, Changning, Youxian, Chaling, Anren, Hengxian, Guidong, Rucheng, Yizhang, Chenxian, Zixing, Guiyang, Xintian, Jiahe, Linwu, Lanshan, Ningyuan, Jianghua, Yongming, Daoxian, and Yangming counties are the bandit suppression zone of the 19th Division, with Division Commander Liu Jianxu as the commander. (3) Xiangtan, Xiangxiang, Anhua, Xinhua, Luxipu, Zhijiang, Huangxian, Qianyang, Huitong, Jingxian, Tongdao, Suining, Chengbu, Xinning, Wugang, and Baoqing counties are the bandit suppression zone of the 16th Division, with Division Commander Luo Fanying as the commander. (4) Nanxian, Huarong, Yuanjiang, Yiyang, Lixian, Anxiang, Cili, Shimen, Linli, Changde, Taoyuan, and Hanshou counties are the bandit suppression zone of the 31st Division, with Division Commander Tao Guang as the commander. (5) Dayong, Chenxi, Luxi, Yuanling, Mayang, Yongshun, Baojing, Longshan, Sangzhi, Guzhang, Qiancheng, Fenghuang, and Yongsu counties are the bandit suppression zone of the First Garrison Headquarters, with Commander Chen Quzhen as the commander. (6) Each unit shall thoroughly eliminate the bandit scourge in each county within its zone, starting from August 1st, with a time limit of two months, and shall also be responsible for supervising and reorganizing the local militias in its zone. Each unit shall carefully plan, assign troops to be responsible for defense and suppression, and report the troop deployment locations and arrival dates, as well as the bandit suppression situation, for record purposes. This order." Currently, Wei Suzhong, commander of the First Zone, entered Pingjiang County on the 22nd and is pursuing the bandit Peng Dehuai. Liu Jianxu, commander of the Second Zone, departed from Changsha for Hengzhou on the 21st to take charge of the suppression. Luo Fanying, commander of the Third Zone, is currently searching for the remnants of Tang Zhemin and Li Zemin in Wugang and has been pursuing them for days. Tao Guang, commander of the Fourth Zone, has arrived in Changde from the province and is drawing troops to suppress He Long in various directions. Chen Quzhen, commander of the Fifth Zone, is currently in Fenghuang and will cooperate with the Fourth Zone to suppress He Long.

He also believes that the bandits Peng, Huang, and He Long have a large following and are spreading throughout Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces. It would be difficult to eliminate them unless the three provinces join forces. Although joint suppression campaigns have been held in the past, they were not effective because no experienced military officers were in charge of commanding the troops of the three provinces. He specially telegraphed Generalissimo Chiang, requesting that He Yingqin be appointed as the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi in order to unify the command and eliminate the bandit scourge. (July 23rd)

○ French Capital Warship

Case of Sailors Assaulting Chinese Sailors 79

Incident Details and Diplomatic Documents

Hankou Correspondence: The French gunboat stationed in Hankou originally had ten Chinese sailors: Zhang Mouqing, Chen Yuancai, He Changfa, Zhang Shaohua, Zhou Yuwen, Zhang Dechao, Zhang Bingquan, Chen Senlin, Zhu Zihui, and Zheng Jingtang. On the evening of the 18th of this month, at 8 PM, they were suddenly and violently beaten by sailors from the same vessel. Furthermore, the first officer of the ship dismissed Zhang and the others, refusing to pay their wages and forcibly disembarking them. Zhang and the others then filed a complaint with the Seamen's Association, seeking relief. After investigation by the Association, the facts were confirmed. A formal letter was sent to Li Fang, the diplomatic inspector of the five provinces, and submitted to the Hankou Municipal Government for forwarding to the French consulate for serious negotiations. It is reported that the Municipal Government has, on the 25th, consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, urging the French side to provide a proper resolution. The following is an excerpt of various documents related to this case:

Petition from Workers: Requesting urgent assistance and rescue. We, the undersigned workers, have been serving as sailors on the French gunboat "Dupleix" for many years. On the evening of July 18th, at 8 PM, we were inexplicably and brutally beaten by the ship's sailors. They even threatened to throw us into the water for amusement. Seeing the sailors' violence and ruthlessness, we had no choice but to seek protection from the ship's first officer in order to save our lives. Unexpectedly, the first officer not only failed to protect us but also said that such trivial matters should not be reported and ordered each of us to pay a fine of one dollar. We argued against this. Seeing our debate, the first officer forced us to leave the ship within five minutes. Seeing that the first officer was determined to suppress us, we requested the ship's interpreter, Yu Fanshi, to ask the first officer to calculate and pay the wages we were entitled to for this month before leaving the ship. However, the first officer stubbornly refused to pay and threw our luggage and bedding into the river. All of the circumstances of the first officer's oppression and mistreatment of us can be testified to by the ship's interpreter, Yu Fanshi, and the kitchen steward. We are deeply concerned that we have been subjected to insults and abuse and denied our wages without any fault on our part. Therefore, we respectfully submit this document, requesting that your association promptly forward it to the Hankou Municipal Government for serious negotiations with the French consulate to maintain our livelihoods and protect our lives. This would be for the public good. (Signed) Zhang Mouqing, Chen Yuancai, He Changfa, Zhang Shaohua, Zhou Yuwen, Zhang Dechao, Zhang Bingquan, Chen Senlin, Zhu Zihui, and Zheng Jingtang, formerly employed on the French gunboat "Dupleix".

Report on Investigation and Reply: Regarding the assigned task of investigating the case of the unjustified dismissal of workers by the first officer of the French gunboat "Dupleix". According to a report from a Mr. Zhou, a chef in the Western kitchen of the "Dupleix" gunboat, at approximately 8 PM on July 18th, French sailors returned to the ship drunk and saw Zhang Dechao, a boy servant of the interpreter Yu, sleeping on the deck of the front cabin. They kicked him and wanted to throw him into the river. Sailors of the ship, unable to bear the situation, tried to dissuade the sailors, which angered them. They then sought out Chinese sailors and beat them severely. To avoid disaster, the sailors had no choice but to report to the first officer, requesting that he stop the violence. Unexpectedly, the first officer sided with the French sailors and rebuked the Chinese sailors for reporting to him, ordering each of them to pay a fine of one dollar; otherwise, they would have to leave the ship within five minutes, and their wages would not be paid. Because the first officer gave the order, the sailors relied on their power to throw the sailors' luggage into the river and expel them from the ship. It is appropriate to report the obtained information truthfully. (Signed) Reporter: Liu Yunqing.

Letter to Li Fang: Dear Sir, Regarding the petition from workers Zhang Mouqing and others, we have dispatched personnel to investigate and report the aforementioned circumstances. In light of this, we have found that the sailors of the "Dupleix" gunboat beat Chinese without cause, and the first officer did not intervene, but instead abused his authority to force the workers to leave the ship and refused to pay them their due wages, throwing away the workers' bedding. This kind of oppressive behavior is sufficient to expose the inferiority of imperialism. In addition to submitting a separate report to the Hankou Municipal Government requesting prompt forwarding for serious negotiations, we hereby send this letter to Your Excellency, the inspector, requesting that you examine the matter and handle it accordingly. We hope for your cooperation. (The letter to the Municipal Government is omitted.) (July 25th)

○ Reorganization of Salt Affairs in Fujian Province

Fuzhou Correspondence: Yang Shuzhuang's return to Fujian this time is intended to first reorganize finances to increase revenue, and it has been decided to start with the reorganization of salt administration. Yesterday, Chen Peikun, He Gonggan, Li Zhiyu, Shen Jinmian, and Chen Erlu, the secretary of the Transportation Office, were specially convened in the Provincial Government Conference Room to discuss ways to reorganize the salt administration for implementation. It is also heard that Transportation Commissioner Shen will go to Beijing in a few days to participate in a salt affairs conference.

During Chen Fu's tenure, the Fujian Salt Smuggling Suppression Team was divided into sixteen large teams, each with three medium-sized teams. After Mr. Liu Xiaoting took over the head of the investigation bureau, he found that the original organization was not in line with the regulations. A few days ago, he ordered the abolition of the large team titles and renamed them battalions, with a total of six battalions, each with three companies. He also ordered the department to draft various opinions for him to take to Beijing to discuss with Minister Song, and he has already packed and is waiting for the boat. (23rd)

○ Zhao Jie Assassinated

Xuzhou Correspondence: Zhao Jie, the younger brother of Zhao Ti, the former governor of Henan, volunteered two months ago, saying that a certain unit in Henan Province used to be under his command and that he could recruit them for our use. Liu Zhi, the commander-in-chief of the Second Army Corps, in order to enlist miscellaneous troops to prevent them from being used by the enemy, presented a request to Generalissimo Chiang to appoint Zhao as the commander of the Garrison Army, with Dong Zhentang as his deputy. The original order was for him to enter Henan to recruit and reorganize. However, Zhao set up his headquarters at the Jiangbei Hotel in Dongguan and appointed Zhang and Sun as commanders of the First and Second Garrison Brigades, ordering them to recruit bandits in the surrounding villages, resulting in the accumulation of bandits such as Cao Chuanjin, who was also appointed as a regimental commander. There were open robberies and secret thefts, and the local area was in turmoil. In May, Zhao was ordered to be transferred to Henan. Zhang's unit, the First Brigade he had recruited, was unwilling to be transferred. The garrison commander of Xuzhou, Song Runtian, together with the county public security team, disbanded the brigade. On the 13th of this month, Cao Chuanjin's bandit unit stationed at Daxujia was ordered to enter Henan, but when they arrived at Donghe Village, they rebelled again and became bandits. Commander-in-chief Liu learned of this and telegraphed the Xuzhou Garrison Command from Yanzhou on the 23rd, stating that, "In order to enlist miscellaneous troops to prevent them from being used by the enemy, this headquarters presented a request to the Generalissimo to approve the appointment of Zhao Jie as the commander of the Garrison Army of this Army Corps and Dong Zhentang as the deputy commander, ordering them to recruit old units in Henan to harass the enemy. Unexpectedly, after being appointed, the commander recruited complex elements in Jiangsu, Shandong, and Anhui provinces and acted improperly. Later, this headquarters discovered this and limited the commander to lead his troops to Zhecheng and Taikang to work. According to reports, most of the troops are now in Xiayi, but some are still staying in Jiangsu, Shandong, and Anhui provinces, refusing to comply with the order to move out. Furthermore, they are recruiting bandits under the guise of pacification, disturbing the local area repeatedly, which is extremely illegal and deeply hateful. In addition to ordering the commander to supervise the troops that have entered Henan to work hard to attack the enemy and ordering the cancellation of the recruitment of those who remain in Jiangsu, Shandong, and Anhui provinces, if anyone else uses the name of the unit to recruit bandits and disturb the area, please order your subordinates to arrest them strictly." A person from Yongcheng said that Zhao Jie's headquarters was located outside Wanghewei in eastern Yongcheng, with about seventy or eighty people. On the 21st, dozens of people in blue military uniforms and civilian clothes broke into Zhao's headquarters, tied up Zhao, and shot him dead with a pistol. The body has now been moved to Dangshan for burial.

○ New Information on the Heinous Murders in Shenyang Shenyang Correspondence: In the case of the heinous murders of eight people in the Li residence in the commercial port area, after the arrest and delivery of Deng Haiquan to the court, several interrogations have not yet revealed the truth. It has recently been learned that the mastermind of the case has been arrested in Beijing and escorted to the Shenyang court. The court is keeping the names of the perpetrators and the details of the arrest secret. However, according to investigations, the culprit's surname is Wang, his given name is Weiguo, and he used to be a section member in a certain institution. Before Deng Haiquan's arrest, when the matter had not been revealed, Wang Weiguo had no intention of escaping. After Deng was arrested, Wang learned the truth and realized that he could not stay in the provincial capital, so he went to Beijing to take refuge temporarily. Wang's home is inside the South Gate. The court and the Public Security Bureau had previously searched it, but there was no evidence. Unexpectedly, after Wang went to Beijing, he missed his wife and sent a letter home, stating that he was living comfortably in a certain place in Beijing and that she should not worry. This letter was intercepted by the police bureau and handed over to the court. Combining this with Deng Haiquan's confession, it was learned that the mastermind had fled to Beijing. The chief prosecutor of the procuratorate of the court, Xue Shuping, and prosecutor Wu Xubin, took the train to Beijing on the evening of the 16th of this month. After arriving in Beijing, they requested assistance from the Beijing police to go to Wang's residence and arrest him immediately. The Beijing Public Security Bureau sent a police officer to escort him to Shenyang. He arrived in Shenyang at 6:40 AM on the 20th, aboard the third special express train. When the suspect got off the train, he was wearing a gray silk long gown and white silk trousers, with handcuffs and shackles. The scene was extremely serious. The car was specially prepared by the court. In addition to the suspect and the driver, there were also two plainclothes officers (the prosecutors) and many police officers escorting him. Observers recognized the suspect, Wang Weiguo, who had worked with the deceased Li Peiqin in the Railway Law Enforcement Office. There was also bloodstained clothing and a large bag of related photos in the car. The cause of the case is no more than two: financial gain and adultery. However, given Wang's position and status, the issue of financial gain is unlikely to be the problem. It is only that Li Peiqin's wife, Shang Lingzhi, used to be a drum singer, and Wang and Peiqin were colleagues. There may have been some relationship between them. (21st)

○ Hangzhou Quick Dispatch

The National Smuggling Suppression Conference will be held in Shanghai on August 1st. Zhen Shaoyao, the director of the Smuggling Suppression Bureau of Zhejiang, has submitted five proposals to the meeting: 1. Supplementary firearms case; 2. Salary increase case; 3. Control of commercial patrols case; 4. Investigation of official transportation case; 5. Increase of long-distance telephone case.

The second phase of the Zhejiang land declaration work, drafted by the Department of Civil Affairs, will begin on August 1st. The departments will organize the survey work in phases and must complete it all by the end of the 23rd year of the Republic.

Zhejiang First Prison will add operations technicians, build workshops, increase funds, and expand operations starting from the 19th year of the Republic. The Hangzhou Municipal Government ordered the Public Works Bureau to plan to set up public wedding halls in four places: Huxin Pavilion, Three Pools Mirroring the Moon, Ruan Gongdun, and Pinghu Qiuyue in West Lake, and an observatory on Geling Mountain.

The long-distance telephone jointly operated by the Ministry of Communications and Zhejiang Province has been disconnected for a long time. Now that both parties have made concessions, the connection will be restored on August 1st.

The Zhejiang Department of Finance recently borrowed 300,000 yuan in short-term loans secured by tobacco tax revenue due to the shortage of government expenses. The Chinese and local banks have already processed it. It is heard that the Ministry is urging the Department to remit the funds urgently, and it is now negotiating with the Bank of China to borrow another 200,000 yuan for remittance, which is expected to be completed in the next few days.

Various industries in Hangzhou City, including silver shops, money houses, silk shops, and pawnshops, are rushing to register. The assistants and employees can all become members and jointly organize industry associations. The registration matters for each industry will be completed by the 3rd of next month, and then the establishment of the association will begin.

Yin Zhengyao, the magistrate of Fuyang County, dispatched police on the 22nd to arrest and detain Yu Baolian, a member of the First District Party Department of the county, and Jin Zhijun, the head of Dali Village. The case is extremely complicated. Jin and others have sent representatives to Hangzhou to file a complaint with the High Court, alleging that the county magistrate illegally arrested them and requesting a transfer of jurisdiction to the Hangzhou District Court for trial. All Sectors Telegraph to Retain District Chief Zhong: The county previously received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs to transfer the district chiefs of the county, including Zhong Taishi, the district chief of the First District, and eleven others, to the province for training, with a deadline of the 25th for reporting. However, upon hearing the news, all sectors in the city are thinking of retaining District Chief Zhong of the First District. Fengxian 81

Dispatch Personnel to Investigate Prison Escape Case: The Fengxian County Prison under the High Court has more than eighty prisoners, mostly bandits and thieves. At approximately 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the 21st, while guard Ding was distributing the prisoners' evening meals, the prisoners suddenly rioted and rushed out of the gate, taking away the guns of the gate guards and the Public Security Bureau, injuring five or six guards. A total of fifty-eight people escaped out of the gate at that time. Prison warden Liu Ou immediately telegraphed the county government. County Magistrate Shen Qingchen personally led the police and the Public Security Bureau chief to pursue the escaped prisoners. The escaped prisoners opened fire to resist arrest, and the police bravely fought back, killing twenty-three escaped prisoners on the spot and capturing thirteen. Twenty-two escaped. County Magistrate Shen immediately ordered the captured escaped prisoners to be taken to the county for detention and telegraphed Prison Warden Liu to the county for questioning about the incident. Because the prison escape was due to the warden's poor management, he ordered the warden to be taken into custody for investigation. Yesterday (26th), he telegraphed High Court President Lin to request instructions. President Lin immediately dispatched Yao Guozhang, the director of the prison section, to Fengxian to investigate and report.

Detailed Account of the Fengcheng Prison Break: Since the early days of the Republic of China, before the current term, the Fengcheng prison has had seven prison breaks, large and small. In the last two years, there have been three in succession. However, the person in charge has been confused and has allowed his subordinates to act illegally and recklessly, resulting in another major case of armed prison break on the 21st. A week before the case, secret meetings had been held repeatedly in the prison, which was learned by Long Shao (a person elected by the veteran prisoners). He secretly reported to the prison officials, but was blamed for spreading rumors. Long Shao was angry and secretly communicated with the prisoners. On the 21st, when Long Shao saw an opportunity, he went to summon the prisoners. So more than a hundred prisoners rushed out during the 4:00 PM mealtime. Most of the shackles had already been destroyed. The prisoners first knocked down the gate guards and robbed their guns. Then they rushed to the Public Security Bureau No. 2 next door to rob guns, and then fired wildly outside, fleeing in all directions from the east and south gates. The Public Security Bureau team stationed there heard the news and pursued them. The escaped prisoners gathered at the east gate and pushed the murderer Wu Liang to lead the way back to resist arrest. The fighting was like a major battle. It is estimated that more than 800 bullets were fired. However, the area was open and close to the coast, resulting in many escapes. The county government was too far away and did not receive the alarm until midnight. County Magistrate Shen led a team of the county police force and Commander Ding Zhiyan with a part of wooden shell guns to suppress the riot and sent officers to search in all directions. County Magistrate Shen personally rewarded the prisoners who did not escape. Yesterday (23rd), the aftermath was properly handled. In addition to reporting the case for instructions, it was determined that the cause of the case was entirely due to the negligence of the prison warden Liu Ou, so he was taken back into custody to await disposal. According to the person in charge, the exact number of escapees was 22, with 12 captured. Including the three prisoners who were found drowned in Xiaohong yesterday, the total number of those who were killed and captured was 27. However, the previous report that many residents were injured by stray bullets was just a rumor and not true.

Nanhui 82

Execution by Firing Squad of Four Bandits: Nanhui County Government Notice: Announcement of Crimes. It has been found that the bandit Zhou Caiqing was captured by the government. According to his confession, he conspired with Wang Wenqi and Shen Xingmin on the night of March 16th of the 18th year of the Republic of China to kidnap Dong Wencai, the grandson of farmer Dong Yuanzhang of Xiasan Jia, Tuan, County, and extorted a ransom. The case has been sentenced to death and reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. The prisoner was taken to the execution ground at 3 PM on the 24th of this month to be identified and executed by firing squad to serve as a warning. Another notice: Announcement of Crimes. According to the Public Security Bureau and the Security Corps, the bandits Feng Xiaodi, Yang Shuigen, and Zhang Asan were captured and sent to the government one after another. According to the interrogation, Feng Xiaodi confessed to conspiring to kidnap Lin Anchun, a doctor from Hengmian. Yang Shuigen confessed to guarding the hostage Yu Genlin. Zhang Asan confessed to jointly rowing the boat. The crimes of the criminals cannot be forgiven and should be sentenced to death. The Jiangsu Provincial Government approved the death sentences for Feng Xiaodi, Zhang Asan, and Yang Shuigen, as there was solid evidence of kidnapping for ransom. Therefore, the prisoners Feng Xiaodi, Yang Shuigen, and Zhang Asan were taken to the execution ground at 10 AM on the 18th of this month to be identified and executed by firing squad to serve as a warning. In addition to reporting, the crimes are hereby announced for public knowledge.

Wuxi 85

Seventy-Seven-Year-Old Man Burned to Death by Thieves: Feng Kunrong, a farmer from Yuxiangzhen, Luoshe, in the 16th District (Wan'an), was seventy-seven years old and in good health, but his hearing was impaired. His eldest son is a skilled chef and is currently working as a chef in Japan. His second son is studying at a university in Shanghai, and his eldest grandson is studying at Soochow Middle School in Suzhou. Unexpectedly, after 1 AM the night before last, seven thieves sailed a small boat to the pier in front of Feng's house. The thieves, holding knives, crowded ashore and first went to rob Feng's neighbor. His daughter-in-law heard the noise and urgently told Kunrong to escape, but Kunrong's hearing was impaired. While he was groping, the thieves had already broken into the house, grabbed Kunrong, and forced him to reveal where the silver was hidden. Kunrong falsely claimed that he was a long-term worker. The thieves were angry at his cunning and found kerosene to pour over Kunrong's body and set him on fire, causing him to be burned all over. They then searched everywhere and took away the loot after an hour. After the incident, his family immediately hired a boat to take Kunrong to the brothers hospital in the city, but he was severely injured and died soon after. His family has already arranged for his coffin and is urging his son to return to Wuxi to handle the funeral and report the incident to the authorities for investigation.

Chamber of Commerce Guns Robbed: After 10 PM the night before last, more than twenty young people took four prostitutes and rode in three water carriages on the Ten Mile Ronghu Lake, enjoying the scenery and laughing loudly all the way. When the boat reached Jiangjiankou, the sentry post of the Chamber of Commerce saw them and suspected them of being bandits. They shone a flashlight on the boat, and the young people suspected that they were intentionally insulting them, so they shouted loudly and then went ashore to make trouble for the Chamber of Commerce, and their guns were robbed. The Chamber of Commerce members rushed to inform Chen Suliang, the commander of the Tenth Detachment, who led all the members to pursue them. The people on the boat were enjoying themselves with the guns they had robbed from the Chamber of Commerce. After Commander Chen asked them, the young people refused to show weakness, and a conflict broke out. In the darkness, they fought for a long time, and both sides were injured. It is heard that some of the young people were wearing uniforms and were members of the police force. Both sides have now reported the details to the county government and requested a thorough investigation. When the two sides were fighting fiercely, the people in Beicheng, who did not know the truth, were greatly shocked because the rumors were flourishing and it was late at night.

He then went to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau outside the Guangfu Gate to spread the same rumors. He was discovered by the bureau, arrested, and interrogated. It is learned that the Suzhou Military Police Regiment Joint Inspection Office recently captured a reactionary criminal, and one Zhu Jicheng escaped. Now it is reported that a Zhu Maoquan in our county claimed to be the head of the regiment and spread rumors and was arrested and interrogated. Director Xu sent the letter to the County Government for clarification before replying.

Barber Arrested for Rape: Shen Bo'an, a resident of No. 17 Jiangyin Lane, outside the North Gate of the county, is blind and makes a living by fortune-telling. His daughter, Qi Zhen (16 years old), is graceful. At 2:30 AM the day before yesterday, Kong Aqiz (19 years old), a barber from the lane, sneaked into Shen Qizhen's room intending to rape her. Shen immediately shouted for help. Aqiz immediately grabbed Shen's throat with his hand. Shen Bo'an heard his daughter's cries and went upstairs to investigate. At the same time, police officer Sun Guilin also heard the cries and went to the scene and saw Kong Aqiz climbing out of Shen's upstairs window. He immediately stepped forward to arrest him and took him to the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Zhou, the director of the branch, held a preliminary interrogation and determined that the case involved rape and immediately transferred him to the general bureau. Yesterday (26th) at 8 AM, he was transferred to the County Government. Zhou, the trial officer, held a trial and ordered Shen Bo'an and Shen Qizhen to return home and detained Kong Aqiz pending trial according to law.

Yangzhou 88

The Twists and Turns of Arresting a Suspected Military Officer: Li Cunde, residing in the city, claimed to have been appointed as the commander of the 2nd Regiment of the 1st Detachment by a certain military guerrilla headquarters some time ago to carry out recruitment duties. The night before, a man claiming to be Secretary Liu of the current 8th Army Guerrilla Headquarters, along with a Mr. Guo, arrested Li Cunde at Huojia Bridge, believing Li to be a fake military officer. They then escorted him to Yangzhou and housed him at the Tiancheng Hotel, intending to transport him elsewhere. However, yesterday (the 24th) at 10 AM, military police inspectors inspecting the hotel suspected that while Li was a suspect, Liu and Guo may also be impersonating military officers. Because the arresters did not have the appropriate official documents, all three were taken to the brigade headquarters for transfer. The headquarters will first detain them and send telegrams to the military units to which each claimed to belong to verify the truth. Further decisions will be made after the responses from the two units arrive in Yangzhou.

Embezzlement of Relief Grain Reported to the County for Investigation: The Sixth District Office of Jiangdu County reported that the Dongguo Township Office and others had stated that during the Minshi (Republic Year 10) flood, the county government issued over thirty dan of rice from the Sino-Foreign Relief Society to aid the people of the township. It has been nine years since then, and the rice has not been distributed. The Fifth District Fourth Branch had sent a letter to Xu Ruizhou, the former chairman of the board of directors, and Yang Tai, the local security officer in charge of the rice at the time. Both replied in writing that Cai Yuquan, the former chairman of the Farmers' Association, had taken the rice. The branch then sent a letter to Cai, setting a deadline for its return. Cai stubbornly denied this. Yesterday, the matter was specially reported to the county government for instructions on how to handle it.

Petition to Move the Address of Wounded Soldiers: The Yaoyang Match Company, located outside the South Gate of the city, was established in the tenth year of the Republic. It has operated intermittently and is now suffering losses and halting production due to competition from Swedish matches. Recently, more wounded soldiers arrived and had nowhere to live, so the factory near the river was temporarily borrowed as a temporary medical residence. All the renovations involved a lot of expenses. The company's supervisor, Mr. Hu Xianbo, specially petitioned the county government to find a way to negotiate a relocation to protect the company's assets.

Continued Transportation of Rice for Sale at a Fair Price: The County Chamber of Commerce, due to the high price of rice and the lack of supply, specially commissioned Wang Jingting to purchase several thousand bags of foreign rice and transport them from Shanghai to Yangzhou for sale at a fair price to maintain the people's food supply. Now that the season of shortage between crops has arrived, another four thousand bags of foreign rice have been transported to Yangzhou. The rice is being sold at the Jinxi Rice Store's large warehouse near Xiangshui Bridge at the South Gate, reducing costs and setting the price at sixteen yuan per dan and three hundred sixty cash per sheng for retail sales. Starting from the 27th of the National Calendar, from 8 AM to 12 PM every morning, buyers can go to the accounting table to pay the price, receive a ticket, and redeem the rice. The ticket will be invalid the next day.

Investigation Ordered into the Removal of the Head of the General Field: Anhui Transport Commissioner Zhang Jiarui reported that Cui, a bandit from Dongtai, had accused Wang Yide, the head of the general field in Taizhou, of corruption, leading to orders for investigation and removal. After secretly investigating the matter, it was discovered that Cui's accusations were false. Therefore, a reply was made to retain Wang. Now, an instruction from superiors has been received, informing them that Cui has again made accusations, urging a well-considered removal of the title of head of the general field and an immediate cancellation of the position of director. It is clear that Cui is making false accusations due to his lack of success. In addition to complying with the order, a trusted official has been specially dispatched to secretly investigate. If the accusations are found to be false, Cui will be arrested and prosecuted for false accusations to deter such improper behavior. As for whether the head of the general field should be removed, it still requires detailed consideration before reporting for approval.

However, when they reached Zhang Bali, the bandit suddenly tried to escape and was killed. His body was displayed on the road for a day.

Pinghu 91

Xielefang Suffers Another Robbery: The home of Shen Peizhen, a farmer in Hujia Marsh, Xiele Village, was broken into by more than ten bandits at midnight yesterday. They looted the house of clothing, bedding, silver, and money, and left after an hour.

Jiangjun Village Has a Sleepless Night Full of Scares: The family of a farmer surnamed Pu in Jiangjun North Village, east of Danjia Bridge, built many houses last year, showing off to others. The other day, at dusk, the family was enjoying the cool air in front of the house when seven or eight people wearing flat-topped straw hats headed straight for the house. The Pu family saw that their actions were frightening and shouted loudly. The villagers gathered, and the people changed their course and left. The Pu family asked the villagers to stay with them overnight.

Huzhou 92

The New County Magistrate Takes Office: Wu Xing County Magistrate Xi Shinong has been in office for two years since his arrival. He was recently transferred to Hangzhou and Haiyan County by provincial order. Li Guangyu, the magistrate of Haiyan County, was transferred to Wuxing. Mr. Li arrived in Huzhou from Hangzhou at 1 PM yesterday and is scheduled to take office at the county government at 9 AM today (the 25th).

Jiaxing 93

Subsidies Issued for Fair Price Sales Losses: Jiaxing has been conducting fair price sales since July 1st for about a month. Rice merchants have been slow to procure rice for fair price sales, so many fair price vouchers are still left in the hands of poor households. The Fair Price Sales Committee has decided to subsidize each dou by two jiao and each dan by two yuan from the county's allocated grain reserves of 15,000 yuan for use. The county government has now decided to distribute the fair price sales loss subsidies starting on August 1st and has issued orders to the fair price sales offices in each district to instruct the rice shops and stores involved in fair price sales to bring their fair price vouchers to the government at that time to receive the loss subsidies. At the same time, the Finance Bureau has been ordered to allocate 10,000 yuan to pay for the Zhuyin Fuhao training courses. The Zhuyin Fuhao Training Course in the Second Middle School District is scheduled to open on July 28th at Jiaxing Second Middle School. Previously, the organizers sent letters to the education bureaus of Jiaxing, Jiashan, Haiyan, Tongxiang, Chongde, Pinghu and other six counties to send personnel to attend and promote the course. The trainees from each county have been assigned by the education bureaus.

Hangzhou 94

Implementing Improvements to Longquan Porcelain Industry: The porcelain produced in Longquan County, Zhejiang Province, is simple, elegant and beautiful in design. Since the Qianlong era of the Qing Dynasty, the wealth of production has been considerable. This year, the Zhejiang Construction Department finalized a plan to improve the porcelain industry and submitted it to the Provincial Government for approval. The original Longquan porcelain kilns will be converted into raw material factories, and a new factory will be established in Yongjia County, which is convenient for transportation, to participate in machine manufacturing and first produce items that meet social needs. It is learned that the Construction Department has already internally determined the candidate for the factory director and will issue an official announcement as soon as the entire budget is approved at the Provincial Government meeting next Monday.

Strictly Prohibit Oppressive Stamp Tax Practices: The Zhejiang Stamp Tax Bureau has received an order from the Ministry of Finance stating that recent investigations have revealed that various sub-bureaus are not operating properly, causing public resentment, or that police officers are assisting in oppressive practices. It is ordered to strictly prohibit these practices and has issued letters to the Public Security Bureau yesterday to investigate and prohibit these practices.

Ningbo 95

Municipal Loan Agreement Established: The Municipal Short-Term Construction Public Bond of 300,000 yuan has been finalized by Mayor Yang through negotiations with various sectors. Yesterday at 3 PM, representatives from the money industry, Zhou Xunzhai and Zhou Yucai, representatives from the banking industry, Rui Zhang, and representatives from the rice industry, Zhuo Baoting, were invited to the General Chamber of Commerce to sign the agreement, officially announcing its establishment.

Prison Official Escapes While in Custody: Zhu Chaolin, the former prison official of Fenghua County, was dismissed and sent to prison to await investigation for releasing a major criminal. However, yesterday morning, due to a slight lapse in supervision by the Public Security Bureau, Zhu Chaolin took the opportunity to escape. By the time they realized and pursued him, he was long gone.

Chunhui Ransom Impossible to Rescue: Fan Shoukang, the principal of Chunhui Middle School in Yiting, teacher Wu Minxing, and student Xia Dingcai were kidnapped by bandits over a month ago. Although the families have repeatedly received letters from the bandits demanding ransom, there is no place to make contact, so they have not yet been rescued. However, according to reports, the bandits are indeed in the Siming Mountains, so Chen Yuhui, the commander of the Second Battalion of the Security Brigade, recently sent troops to the mountains to rescue them. However, the mountains are unusually steep, and the bandits are long-time residents and familiar with the terrain. By the time the soldiers arrived, they had already moved with the hostages, making it impossible for the soldiers to rescue them. They returned to camp yesterday and reported their mission.

Shangyu 96

Investigating the Bribery Case of Trial Officer and Tobacco Offender: The County Party Department's Propaganda Department disclosed in a current affairs briefing at 2 PM that "a prison officer colluded with judicial personnel to extort 185 yuan from tobacco offender He Baoqing and has been prosecuted." This short news item was known to Trial Officer Zhu Yao, who believed that since this matter involved collusion and bribery between administrative and judicial personnel, it should not be ignored. He decided to conduct a thorough investigation. At the same time, public opinion generally suspected Kong Gongxian, a record keeper in the county government. The findings of the investigation are recorded as follows: Previously, the Baiguan Public Security Branch arrested a current tobacco offender named He Baoqing last month and handed him over to the county government. After interrogation, he was found guilty of both trafficking and smoking tobacco and sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Later, He's family hired a local gentry and retired bailiff Chen Changshou to bribe Kong with 185 yuan to arrange for his release. Later, He requested to seek treatment outside of the jail, claiming to be seriously ill. Trial Officer Zhu approved it because he realized that this happened during summer and not allowed it. Thus, He's family and Chen Changshou, due to Kong's ineffectiveness, not only threatened Kong with prosecution to recover the 185 yuan but also spread rumors about the bribery process, which was then exposed and conveyed to a certain cadre in the County Party Department, hence the item on the briefing. Zhu was extremely indignant after hearing the news and photographed the briefing on the 22nd to keep as evidence. He also sought clues to the case in the hope of uncovering the truth.

Xiaoshan 97

Accidental Shooting Case Scheduled for Trial: In the case where Chen Xijiu, an investigator in the Xiaoshan County Public Security Bureau, accidentally shot and killed guard Guo Yongxiang while cleaning his gun, the deceased's father and brother had already submitted a request to the county court to close the case after mediation. However, Prosecutor Yang had already investigated the case and filed a lawsuit, so it was not approved. It is heard that the case is scheduled to be heard on August 2nd for further verification and judgment.

Reduced Tobacco Leaf Harvest: Sidu in Xiaoshan has always been a tobacco-producing area, and the annual income is considerable. However, this year, the area was affected by a windstorm that blew the crops down, followed by the prevalence of pestilence, causing the withered plants to die everywhere. The general laboring farmers are quite worried.

Sports 98

○ Davis Cup First Day Final

The United States and France Each Win a Singles Match

The United States' Tilden Wins 3-1 Against France's Borotra

France's Cochet Wins 3-0 Against the United States' George Lott

(Paris Dispatch, 25th) The Davis Cup, which has been the focus of global attention in recent years, has become a contest between the United States and France. In 1925 and 1926, the United States lost twice to France, which held the championship. Since 1927, France, with the strength of the Four Musketeers, has seized the world championship and continued to maintain it in 1928 and 1929. Now, the players from the United States and France have met again at the Auteuil Stadium in Paris, France. July 25th was the first day for the two countries to compete for friendship and championship. The result of the day was that the United States and France each won a singles match.

(1) Tilden is Strong and Vigorous, Winning 3-1 99

French Player Dominates: At the start of the first set, France's Borotra performed excellently, displaying all his superb skills. The veteran Tilden from the United States was unable to support it and was defeated by the opponent with a score of 6-2 in the first set, which seemed to be no difficulty.

Veteran Seizes Opportunity: The veteran has been on the battlefield for a long time, with a calm will. The cannonball-like serve constantly attacked the French player, occupying an excellent advantage. Borotra succumbed to the veteran's power and lost the second and third sets with scores of 5-7 and 4-6.

Final Effort: The French player initially struggled in the fourth set but made efforts to catch up, which was very exciting. The audience was amazed. Starting with a 1-4 deficit, he gradually came to life through his indomitable struggle. While resisting the veteran's formidable抽擊(chou ji) serve, he calmly seized the opportunity to counterattack and reached a 5-5 tie. It was not easy. Unfortunately, the veteran managed to win the last two games. The veteran won the fourth set with a score of 7-5. In total, the United States' Tilden won with a score of 3-1.

Tilden (United States) 100

Borotra (France) 101

(2) Cochet Achieves Smooth Success 102

Winning 3-0

Recovering from Adversity: France's Cochet won straight sets with scores of 6-4, 6-2, and 6-2 against the United States' Lott. However, at the beginning of the match, the French player was quite careless, giving the opponent a 4-3 lead, which caused dissatisfaction among the French fans in the audience. Fortunately, the French player rallied in time and recovered from adversity, finally winning with a score of 6-4.

Sweeping the Army: Since the first set, Cochet has shown great power, with amazing 抽繫(chou xi) and shocking interceptions, making the American player unable to cope. As a result, the French player won the second and third sets with scores of 6-2 and 6-2. In total, Cochet won with a score of 3-0.

Cochet (France) 103

Lott (United States) 104

52-26 against Shanghai University Team

○ Explanation from the Ministry of Education

Measures for Private Junior High School Students to Enter Higher Schools 108

The Ministry of Education explained that private junior high school graduates who are not registered may be admitted to senior high schools if they are of comparable level and pass the examination. The Zhejiang Department of Education was informed by telegram that Article 17 of the Provisional Regulations for Middle Schools stipulates that "the qualifications for admission to senior high schools are graduation from junior high school. If they do not have the above qualifications but are of comparable level and pass the examination, they may also be admitted." Private junior high school graduates who are not registered may be admitted to senior high schools if they are of comparable level and pass the examination, and there is no need to set up a separate preliminary examination for admission. However, they must comply with the Ministry's No. 854 Instruction of the previous year ("Strictly Regulate the Admission Qualifications of Enrolled Students"). All levels of schools should strictly handle the enrollment of students. The qualifications for admission to colleges and universities must be graduation from senior high schools or equivalent schools, and students with equivalent academic qualifications may not be admitted. The qualifications for admission to secondary schools must be handled in accordance with Article 17 of the Provisional Regulations for Middle Schools promulgated by the former University Council. The measures to restrict those with equivalent academic qualifications should be strictly stipulated by the universities in each university district, the provincial education departments, or the special municipal education bureaus according to local conditions in order to ensure verification. The Department will stipulate the ratio of this type of student to the total number of newly admitted students.

Local News

Railway Bureau Takes Precautions 117

The police departments of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways telegraphed the chiefs of various sections yesterday, stating: "We have received a secret order from the Administration Bureau, roughly stating that the anniversary of the August 1st Uprising is approaching, and we must strictly guard against the Communists taking the opportunity to demonstrate and disrupt public order. During the current period of military operations at the front, it is imperative to strengthen rear protection. These two railways are important transportation routes, and all bridges and tracks along the line must be strictly guarded. We order the chiefs of each section to increase patrols day and night, strictly prevent and guard against any negligence, and ensure safety, etc." Upon receiving this order, in addition to distributing it, the police chief was instructed to lead all police officers to be armed and patrol in shifts, day and night, and strictly prevent and guard against any negligence.

Turkish Reporter Travels to Various Eastern Countries and Passes Through Shanghai 119

Visited This Newspaper Yesterday for a Week

Scheduled to Take a Ship to Japan at the End of This Month

Mr. Meng Xinni, a reporter for the Turkish Ikada Life Daily, set off from Paris, France, in June to travel to Eastern Egypt, India, the South Sea Islands, and other places to investigate the political and social conditions of the East. He arrived in Shanghai a few days ago for a short rest and will take a ship to Japan on the 30th before heading to the United States for about three months before returning to Constantinople. Yesterday afternoon, Mr. Meng, accompanied by Lu Zhongxiang and others, visited this newspaper. According to him, the greatest impression he gained from his travels to various Eastern countries was the awakening of the Eastern people and their efforts towards freedom and independence, and he firmly believes that they will soon succeed. He had originally planned to meet Gandhi during his stay in India, but ultimately failed to do so. Given the current spirit of the Indian people, he believes that Britain will ultimately be unable to completely suppress them, and at the very least, it should be like Egypt, acknowledging India's independence while Britain maintains a supervisory role. Finally, he said that today's China is similar to the former Turkey, and without the abolition of unequal treaties, it will never achieve liberation. He hopes that the Chinese government and people will unite and strive to achieve final victory.

News of the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike Yesterday 122

Central Government Sends Personnel to Investigate

Four Statements from the French Concession

The Union Refuses to Accept

Huadong News reports that the expansion of the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike is becoming increasingly serious. The factory has consistently shown no sincerity in resolving the issue, making it difficult for mediators and preventing the restoration of traffic in the French Concession. The news from yesterday is recorded again below:

Central Government Attitude: Yang Qingyuan, previously sent by the Municipal Party Department to the Central Government for reporting, has now returned to Shanghai. To understand the Central Government's handling of this matter, a reporter interviewed Comrade Chen Junyi, a member of the Standing Committee of the People's Training Association. According to him, Comrade Yang reported to the Central Party Department upon arriving in Beijing and had a discussion with Central Committee members Chen Lifu, Chen Guofu, and Shi Weihuan of the Central Party Department. The meeting took place on Thursday, the day of the Central Party Department's regular meeting. The Central Committee was very attentive to this matter and immediately decided on two measures: (1) Regarding the tragedy, the Central Committee will forward it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate and protest with the French Ambassador. (2) Regarding the labor strike, the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, the People's Training Association, and the Shanghai Municipal Government are responsible for handling it together. In order to understand the occurrence and current situation of this matter, the Central Committee specially sent Comrade Wang Xingzhou to Shanghai to investigate, so that future negotiations can be carried out. Comrade Wang met with Yu at the People's Training Association yesterday morning and gave a detailed report on the progress. It is also heard that the Central Committee has specially asked Central Committee member Li Shizeng to handle everything nearby.

French Concession Statement: Since the union gave a warning and the Municipal Government sent Secretary Geng to negotiate, the French Concession has not been as dismissive as before. In recent days, it has been studying the various conditions one by one and has made four statements: (1) Wages will be paid for the strike period. (2) Regarding the issue of wage increases, it verbally acknowledges an increase of three yuan per person. (3) It expresses acceptance in principle regarding the tragedy. (4) Workers must return to work according to a list provided by the factory, and more than a hundred workers must be dismissed. The above statements are a response to the warning received by the French Concession.

Union Rejects: The union is extremely indignant about the above four statements from the French Concession and absolutely refuses to accept them. The dismissal of more than a hundred workers is particularly outrageous. This labor movement is exceptionally just, and to dismiss so many workers simply because of the strike is tantamount to a complete failure of the labor movement. Moreover, the French Concession requires the implementation of the four conditions to wait until after the resumption of work, making its intentions even more unpredictable. Therefore, they would rather persist to the end and wait for the resolution of the Central Government and the authorities.

Economic Assistance: The support associations of various labor unions have been discussing their work busily in recent days. It has been decided to donate art to relieve the striking workers of the Water and Electricity Union, and a special report has been submitted to the Municipal Party Department for approval. It is now known that the Municipal People's Training Association has replied, approving the donation and instructing them to negotiate separately with each association and collect a donation fee of one dime per person when collecting membership fees from each labor union to provide relief to the striking workers of the French Concession Water and Electricity Union. In addition to sending a letter to the Social Affairs Bureau for reference, they should be informed, etc. After receiving the approval, the support association immediately raised shares and actively solicited donations.

Shao Ziying Reports: Shao Ziying went to the union yesterday morning to defend himself against the destruction of the labor movement and flattering the capitalists, and asked the union to conduct a strict investigation. If the facts are true, he is willing to accept the spittle of all workers.

Vehicle Affairs Meeting: The workers of the vehicle affairs department held a meeting yesterday, chaired by Wang Jun. Because the work has been complicated recently, six external staff members were publicly elected to carry out all affairs, namely: Xie Xinyu and Gu Peizhi as consultants, Mao Jinquan and Zhao Chunfang as inspectors, and Shen Chunfu and Chen Youjie for transportation. It was also resolved that (1) Those inspectors and ticket writers of Numbers 2 and 5 and other outdoor workers who have not yet reported should be gathered by various means. (2) The outdoor Numbers 3 and 23 ticket inspectors who continue to work in the factory after joining the union are obviously undermining the labor movement and should be warned to report to the meeting within a time limit, otherwise they will be dealt with uniformly. (3) It was decided to promote □□ (illegible) to organize the vehicle affairs, driving and ticketing sections in order to promote unity.

Staff Meeting: Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., more than 180 staff members held a meeting, chaired by Xing Wenrong. It was resolved that (1) In accordance with the resolution of the general meeting, the association will send a letter to the comprador, requiring the staff to resign from their positions and report to the meeting within three days, otherwise appropriate measures will be taken. (2) If any staff members join the strike and still go to the company to work, they should be dealt with severely as a warning to others. (3) Those who have not yet submitted donations should be collected by the team leaders as soon as possible.

Strike Committee Resolves Important Cases: The French Concession Water and Electricity Union held a strike committee meeting yesterday morning at 10 a.m. Chairman Feng Zhiming first reported (omitted). Subsequently, the following was discussed: (1) Shao Ziying has already joined the strike and has been certified by loyal workers as not being a lackey, please review the case. It was decided to consult the support association to review and withdraw the reply. (1) Regarding the lawsuit against Chen Maolin for a check of 1,000 yuan, Chen Maolin is now requesting lawyer Chen Ruilin to come forward and claim that the money is currently deposited in the Siming Bank, but cannot be transferred until January of next year, and all litigation costs should be borne by the association. How should it be handled? It was decided to ignore it and let the law resolve it. (1) Regarding the expansion of the transportation team, it was decided to expand it immediately and send a team to serve the support association. (1) Regarding the release of arrested workers, it was decided to send a letter to the Chinese directors and the legal community to seek relief.

Accurate Number of Strikers: The association had already listed the number of strikers at 1,200 yesterday. After a detailed investigation, the number of original staff and workers working in the factory and the number of people who have now joined the strike are listed separately below: (1) Of the more than 700 workers in the machine affairs department, all have gone on strike. (2) Of the 240 vehicle affairs department drivers, 180 have joined the strike. Of the original 350 ticket sellers, 300 have joined the strike. Of the original 92 outdoor inspectors, ticket inspectors, and ticket writers, 82 have joined the strike. (3) Of the original 200 company staff, 570 have now joined the strike. Combining the above figures, there are approximately 1,600 staff and workers serving the water and electricity company, and 1,430 have now joined the strike front. It is heard that there are still many people rushing to report, it is said.

Taxpayers' Association Sends Telegram: The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday, stating: "To Minister Wang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government in the Capital: Since the outbreak of the labor strike at the French Concession Water and Electricity Company, the company has not known how to eliminate the crisis in an honest manner, but has been trying to expand the situation. This is not only betting the reputation and business of the French company on a single stake, but also endangering local safety. If unfortunate events occur during this period, causing unexpected suffering to the people, the company should be absolutely responsible. Moreover, the company earns millions in surplus every year, and is willing to use a small portion of the surplus to control the lives of workers, causing hundreds of thousands of citizens who rely on the French Concession for their livelihood to live in constant fear. The French Concession authorities, which have the ability to stop this, have hardly taken any measures to eliminate it, which is difficult to understand. Therefore, it is said that the French Concession Water and Electricity Company has the support of the Paris headquarters, and although it absolutely uses monopoly methods to deal with the Chinese, no one will come forward to uphold justice. Their words are not false. Although the French Concession police have been exceptionally strict in their defenses recently, the company has maintained a calm attitude, and the cost of these defenses is considerable, which will likely be borne by municipal expenses in the future, adding another unnecessary burden on our citizens. How can we remain silent? It is also reported that the French Concession Water and Electricity Company, since obtaining the patent rights, has set water and electricity rates higher than any other water and electricity company, especially water rates. It is now found that the population of the French Concession has increased from less than 100,000 to more than 400,000, and the company's operating income has also increased year by year. This association has repeatedly stated that the company should reduce and equalize water and electricity prices, but it has turned a deaf ear. However, public utilities should be based on the public interest and should not be controlled by a single monopolistic company. If this monopoly continues, our civic groups must rise up and demand correction, and if necessary, propose to the local government to take it back to comply with the principles of public utilities. In addition to sending a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government to raise questions nearby, we are specially telegraphing your department to negotiate with the French Ambassador in order to resolve the situation quickly and calm people's minds (omitted). Chairman Cheng Zhusun and Shang Mu Jiang of the Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association, respectfully inquire."

Stores Must Adhere to the Gregorian Calendar for Hiring and Firing Employees 123

Instructions from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce

The Municipal Government of this city received a consultation from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday, stating that the use of the lunar calendar was banned long ago, but various stores in Shanghai still use the lunar calendar festivals as the standard for hiring and firing employees, disregarding the law. Please instruct the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to inform all businesses and factories that they must adhere to the Gregorian calendar for hiring and firing employees and must not continue to use the lunar calendar, otherwise it will not be effective. The Municipal Government approved the consultation and has already instructed that letters be sent to ensure compliance.

Workers at the Yingchang Factory Went on Strike Yesterday 124

Tong Zhaosan, a worker in the topping room of the Shanghai Yingchang Factory of the Great China Match Company in Lujiazui, Pudong, was frequently taking leave recently. When he asked for leave again yesterday morning between 8 and 9 a.m., he was not approved. Tong could not help but express his dissatisfaction and was fired by the factory. The workers in the room were indignant and suddenly made a commotion. At the same time, workers in other rooms heard the news and responded, leading to a factory-wide strike. The workers then closed the east and west gates tightly, preventing all factory staff from leaving and without food. However, the workers gathered in the factory and maintained order. The factory union reported the incident to the local 5th District Party Department, which sent personnel to mediate. The workers also raised the issue of providing adequate severance pay to the dismissed workers, demanding the factory's acknowledgement. One issue turned into two, and no resolution was reached. Shortly after, representatives from the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau successively sent representatives to the factory to mediate. In the afternoon at 5 p.m., the Municipal Public Security Bureau also sent Inspector Zhang to Pudong to investigate for review and handling. However, as of 7 p.m. last night, the factory gates were still guarded by workers, preventing others from entering or leaving, it is said.

National Government Strictly Investigates Red Cross Case 129

Ordering the Chairman to Expose the Violent Rioters

Standing Committee Members Responsible for Exercising Powers

During the previous Third General Meeting of Members of the Chinese Red Cross, some malicious elements attempted to control the organization for their own gain, instigating rioters to wield weapons and cause chaos at the meeting, and to smash the general office. The National Government ordered the Shanghai Municipal Government to send the Director of the Health Bureau, Hu Hongji, to investigate. After investigation, a report was submitted and suggestions for handling the aftermath were made. Later, the National Government ordered the chairman of the board of directors to expose the violent rioters for legal action. The Health Bureau repeatedly urged the chairman of the board to fully expose the rioters, but he made many excuses. Considering the facts at the time and his legal status, and the fact that Chairman Wang attended every meeting and obeyed every order, he could not shirk his responsibility for providing evidence. He was still urged to quickly make the exposure, but he still procrastinated. The progress of the supervision was reported and submitted to the Municipal Government for instructions, which were forwarded to the National Government. The National Government ordered that the City Government should still be responsible for ordering a speedy exposure and strict supervision, without any leniency. Previously, it was stated that Jiang Qudan should be ordered to cease his duties as a standing committee member because he was considered the initiator of the riot. The City Government should thoroughly investigate and report. As for the handling of the aftermath in the previous report, items two, four, five, and six should be followed by the Municipal Government. Item three should be notified by the Standing Committee for compliance. The Municipal Government has ordered the Health Bureau to comply and report back after thorough implementation. The Municipal Health Bureau sent a letter to the Standing Committee of the association, stating briefly that, in addition to the matter of exposing the rioters who committed violence and created chaos, the chairman, Wang Peiyuan, had already been re-urged to be responsible for the exposure in accordance with the previous orders. Another letter was sent to the assets committee member Huang Hanqi to forward to all committee members to investigate and create a property catalog and expense income and expenditure calculations for separate reporting. A corresponding letter was also sent to your association (1) Immediately convene a meeting to discuss and determine the election rules for standing committee members and the rules of procedure for the members' congress, and other regulations. (2) Immediately notify the branches of the Red Cross by the Standing Committee to convene branch members' congresses to nominate representatives to attend the temporary members' congress on schedule (should be notified separately by telegram or registered mail for verification). Branch representatives must bring official letters bearing the branch's seal when attending. (3) Notify the Red Cross General Office to prepare all the procedures for the temporary members' congress in accordance with general meeting procedures and established regulations, so as to avoid further complications. (5) Before the temporary congress is convened, the current standing committee members, Jiang Qudan, should immediately cease his duties as a standing committee member. It is hoped that you will investigate and handle separately and reply for reporting. Another letter was sent to the Chairman, saying (above omitted) Regarding the exposure of the rioters who wielded weapons to cause chaos at the Third Members' Congress of the Red Cross and smashed the Red Cross General Office, the National Government again ordered that you be ordered to urge the chairman of the board to expose them quickly, and ordered strict supervision without any leniency. A special letter is hereby sent to you, hoping that you will investigate and fully expose within five days of receiving this letter for forwarding to the examination and handling. Otherwise, you will have to truthfully report and request the final sanction. Please do not procrastinate again. And separate letters were sent to the President and Vice President of the Red Cross for review and to the Assets Committee for review. The original letters requesting investigation of assets are omitted here. Now, the five opinions approved by the National Government for the aftermath of the association are excerpted as follows: Item 1: Electing standing committee members is an important event for members to exercise their rights. Election rules should be established and there must be certain procedures in place for deliberations to avoid unnecessary disputes. The detailed rules of procedure should also be formulated quickly for common adherence and to prevent disputes. The current standing committee members should be held responsible for formulating various rules in accordance with Article 31, Paragraph 4 of the association's articles of association, and submit the detailed rules of procedure and election rules for standing committee members for verification and filing, so that they can be used as a reference when convening the members' congress in the future. Item 4: Notify the Red Cross President's Office that all procedures for the temporary congress of members must be prepared in accordance with general practice and the association's various regulations to avoid further incidents. Item 5: Instruct the association to request the government to send personnel to the congress to supervise it daily to show solemnity. Item 6: Before the temporary congress of members is convened, the original standing committee members shall be responsible for exercising supervisory powers, and the assets committee shall, together with the chairman of the board, prepare a property catalog and an expenditure and income calculation report for all assets and income and expenditures of the association, and report to the congress, and report to the government and the competent authorities at the location of the general office in accordance with the legal meaning of Article 10 of the Law on Supervision of Charitable Organizations for record (note) The above four well-meaning opinions have been approved by the National Government and ordered by the Municipal Government to comply. Item 2: The government will issue a notice to local governments across the country to order local Red Cross branches to convene branch members' congresses to nominate representatives to attend the temporary congress on schedule to avoid a lack of quorum. Branch representatives must bring an official letter bearing the branch's seal to prevent imposters (note) The above well-meaning opinion was approved by the National Government and ordered by the Standing Committee of the Association to notify compliance. The Standing Committee should immediately notify the Red Cross branches everywhere to comply.

Hua Lun Resumes Service on the South Sea Route 130

Chinese Goods Only Loaded on Chinese Merchant Ships

Large Sums of Money Transported to Hong Kong

No Foreign Ships Loaded Yesterday, a certain shipping company in this port received a telegram from Xiamen stating that the route from Shanghai to Xiamen and Hong Kong has recently been monopolized by foreign merchants, and they have adopted high-pressure tactics for Chinese merchants' passengers and goods, with little accommodation. The various merchant guilds in Xiamen now have extremely bad feelings with the various foreign shipping companies, and it has been decided that Chinese goods will automatically stop loading on foreign merchant ships in an invisible way.

Gold Awaiting Shipment to Shanghai Since the implementation of the ban on the export of gold, customs has strictly inspected ships leaving for Japan and other ports, resulting in fewer outflows of gold from Shanghai recently. Xiamen currently has a large batch of gold. According to a telegram, there are as many as 3,000 boxes urgently needing to be transported to Hong Kong for re-export overseas. The route has not been specified, but because the transshipment export is unwilling to entrust foreign ships to load, a ship is specially requested to be sent from Shanghai for transportation. Please restore the Chinese shipping route from Shanghai, Xiamen, and Hong Kong. There were originally three regular Chinese ships on this route, but they have been suspended for a long time due to the current situation. The business on this route has been entirely taken over by foreign British and Japanese shipping companies. Now, the various merchant guilds in Xiamen have telegraphed the Shanghai Chinese Shipping Company to restore the South Sea route to meet passenger needs, and have requested that a ship be sent first within the next day or two. Yesterday, it was heard that one Chinese ship would be allowed to resume service from next week.

Meeting of the Shanghai Municipal Council 131

The Shanghai Municipal Council held a board meeting on Wednesday (23rd) to discuss various cases, the more important of which included the publication of the Chinese Municipal Council Gazette and the addition of primary schools in the Western District. Regarding the publication of the Chinese Gazette, the board accepted the proposal of the Chinese directors that the Chinese Taxpayers' Association should be entrusted with the appointment of representatives in the future, and the expenses would be paid by the Municipal Council. As for the sections mentioned by the Director-General of the Municipal Council that translators would need to be added and office space would need to be increased in the future, it was decided that they would be submitted to Clerk for preparing a concrete plan and would be proposed for discussion when the board meeting was convened after the summer vacation. Subsequently, the proposal for the Low-Priced Rice Committee was put forward, and Yuan Ludeng was elected to attend as a representative of the Municipal Council, and it was decided that the Municipal Council would allocate 100,000 yuan for rice purchases. Then, the Chinese directors' proposal that primary schools in the Western District urgently need to be opened, and that No. 84 Avenue Edward VII be temporarily rented for one year before the school buildings are completed for the purpose of opening school was considered. The meeting passed, but it must wait for the Bureau of Works and the Fire Department to send personnel to inspect whether the houses are suitable for school buildings before a final decision can be made.

French Concession Police Continue 132

Warning Shops to Add Stamp Duty

The two commissioners of the French Concession Stamp Duty Office, Liu Chunpu and Shen Rulin, previously found that twelve shops, including Lao Qinghe Silver Store, in the French Concession did not affix stamp duty to their invoices, so they were reported by the General Office and sent to the French General Patrol Room. Considering that it was the first offense, the patrol room sent police officers to warn each household. Yong Tai Xiang Department Store, Xie Da Xiang Foreign Goods Store, Hong Shun Tai Tea Store, De Kang Xing Ji Ying Goods Store, and Tian Fu Run Socks Factory were also summoned by the French Concession Police for not affixing stamp duty to their invoices and were severely reprimanded, and ordered to affix all items that should be affixed with stamp duty within two days. Otherwise, they would be sent to the public office for interrogation. The shops have all formally sent letters to Liu Chunpu and Shen Rulin, the two commissioners of the French Concession Stamp Duty Office, to beg for forgiveness, and the shops have separately purchased stamp duty. The other shops have also heard the news and have rushed to the French Concession Stamp Duty Office to purchase and affix them.
