All Police Students Studying in Japan Depart for Home 134

Arriving in the Next Few Days

Our country has always lacked police officers. In order to train senior police officers, the Ministry of Internal Affairs specially sent police students to study in Japan this spring, stipulating an annual fee of 33,000 yuan. However, due to the soaring price of gold, the original amount allocated was insufficient, and the internal economy was also poor, so it was impossible to maintain the lives of the students in Japan. Moreover, because the students sent did not know Japanese, the benefits obtained were very few. Now, the Executive Yuan has approved the Ministry of Finance to allocate 2,000 yuan for travel expenses and ordered all students in Japan to return home. The travel expenses have been remitted by Wang Rongbao, the Chinese ambassador to Japan, for the students to collect. It is now known that the group of more than 30 people has departed from Japan and is expected to arrive in port in the next few days to report to Beijing and wait for internal arrangements.

Japanese Cultural Inspection Group Arrives in Shanghai 135

Departing from Nagasaki Tomorrow

Arriving in Port on the 30th

According to news from the External Affairs Office in Shanghai, the Far East Cultural Inspection Group organized by the Japanese Daito Bunka Gakuin is scheduled to depart from Nagasaki tomorrow (28th) and arrive in Shanghai on the afternoon of the 30th. The group consists of twelve people and plans to stay in Shanghai for two or three days after arriving in Shanghai. They plan to first visit the Shanghai-Hangzhou line for inspection, and then go to Nanjing. After the Shanghai-Hangzhou and Shanghai-Ningbo lines are completed, they will take a boat from Shanghai to Dalian, Qingdao, and the Liaoning area for inspection. The return date is around August 20th.

Chairman Director Wu Wenhua After the meeting, he performed the ceremony. First, the chairman reported (1) The road surface and bridge projects of the North River Road will be started soon. Due to various technical reasons, it is difficult to erect according to the route. In addition to instructing the staff to be careful in their work and not to damage farmland, the committee has been replied to for investigation. The following resolutions were passed (1) The County Party Affairs Consolidation Committee's letter sending a donation book for the martyrs' pension and requesting assistance in soliciting donations. It was resolved that all staff of the bureau would voluntarily donate according to their ability (2) The Construction Department's order to thoroughly investigate whether the maps of the Changmin Road measured by the former Director Zhang are suitable for reporting was approved. It was resolved to hand it over to the Highway Department for prompt investigation and reporting (3) The County Government's instruction that the National Road Association be approved to transfer the mileage and funding plan of the automobile route from Minhang to Pinghu for proper discussion and reporting was approved. It was resolved to send a letter to the Construction Bureaus of Fengxian, Jinshan, and Pinghu counties for nearby investigation (4) The Construction Department's order to issue a colored marking method for road conditions should be handled. It was resolved that it would be handled jointly by the Technology Section and the Highway Department (5) The application for appropriation of funds for the reconstruction of Tangwan Town streets was submitted. Now, the Construction Department's instruction that the requested appropriation of funds is not convenient to approve should be replied to. It was resolved to send a letter to the second district for investigation.

Vessels Arriving from Cebu Must Be Quarantined 136

Our country has not yet established a special seaport quarantine agency. All previous seaport quarantine affairs were handled by the Customs. Since the establishment of the Ministry of Health in 1928, health experts have been hired from the Health Department of the League of Nations to investigate the seaport quarantine situation in various places in China. Dr. Wu Liande was then sent to prepare for the takeover of national seaport quarantine affairs and the takeover of Shanghai seaport quarantine affairs. Dr. Wu has been preparing in Shanghai for several months, and it is heard that the progress is very smooth. It is also heard that the ministry recently issued an order to receive a report from the Eastern Branch of the Health Department of the League of Nations in Singapore that cholera is epidemic in Cebu, Philippines, so it is designated as an epidemic area in accordance with the regulations of the Seaport Quarantine Regulations. All ships arriving in Shanghai from Cebu, Philippines, shall be subject to inspection and verification.

○ Reorganization of the South Shanghai District Guard Corps News Registration Date Expired Yesterday

Members Are Strictly Selected

After the reorganization and revision of the system of the South Shanghai District Guard Corps of this city, the original twelve teams were merged into nine teams, and then the registration and testing of the members began. It is heard that the registration date expired yesterday and will not be extended. More than 700 people have performed the duties. Those with unhealthy bodies who have already registered will be cut off, and those who are qualified will be assigned to teams according to the distance. In short, the purpose of this reorganization and revision is to seek the soundness and enrichment of the strength of each team. Provisional Measures for Artificial Silk Freight 138

The Vehicle Affairs Offices of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways yesterday notified the forwarding companies of the two railways, saying that they had received a letter from the Management Bureau stating that, according to the order of the Ministry, the freight for artificial silk and artificial silk fabrics carried by passenger cars on the railway should still be charged according to silk fabrics for the time being. After the freight rates committee reviews and stipulates the freight rates for artificial silk, they will be ordered to comply. Therefore, a notice is hereby issued that all artificial silk and artificial silk fabrics handed over to the passenger cars of the two railways for transportation as packages shall be charged according to the silk fabric freight rates stipulated in Article 9, Paragraph 3 of the Transportation Rules for Passenger Cars of the two railways, that is, 50% of the ordinary package freight rate shall be charged. Please comply accordingly.

The Court Orders a Ban on Boy-Girl Dramatic Performances 141

In the case of the dancer Huang Baiying being forced to take poison by Tong Sanmao, after the Special District Local Court sentenced Tong to two years in prison, it temporarily came to an end. The drama industry believes that the plot of this case is very tortuous. At first, it was romantic and unrestrained, and then the love sea was surging, creating a love triangle, which was extremely sad. Shanghai stage sought to be one step ahead and paid attention to collecting all the materials at the beginning of the case. When Tong Sanmao was convicted, it did not wait for its confirmation and published the advertisement that the stage would perform the play in the newspaper, naming it Tong Sanmao and a Certain Dancer, and choosing to premiere on the evening of the 26th. However, Tong deeply unwilling that his romantic affairs would be spread by the actors, he specially hired the two lawyers who defended him, Liu Shifang and Zou Yu, to petition the Special District Court on the 25th to issue an order to prohibit the stage from performing. Now Tong has hired a lawyer to petition for an order to prohibit it, which is of course approved and enforced. Misunderstanding Erupts into Conflict Between Wusong Land and Water Police 142

Fortunately, the Storm Did Not Widen

Both Sides are Willing to Peace

Zheng Zhichuan, a patrolman from the First Police Station of the Seventh District of the Wusong West City Public Security Bureau, was on duty at the entrance of Letian Teahouse on Waimalu at 6:00 PM the day before yesterday. He saw a fisherman carrying a large bundle of fishing nets passing by. The patrolman, fearing that there were smuggled items inside, ordered him to put down the nets for inspection. At that time, several plainclothes water police officers from the Third Platoon of the 16th Team of the 4th District of the Water Police and passers-by stepped forward to watch. The patrolman, fearing that it would hinder traffic, stopped the audience, which led to a conflict with the water police. Then, the water police forced the patrolman to go on board to argue. Because the Third Platoon's gunboat was anchored below Tongxing Wharf, the patrolman had no choice but to follow the crowd on board. Unexpectedly, several patrolmen on shift change were coming from west to east and had not reached Tongxing Wharf. They mistakenly heard from passers-by that the patrolman had been dragged away and beaten by the water police, so the police, upon hearing this, loaded their bullets and rushed to the boat. The water police also moved a small steel cannon installed on the bow of the boat in preparation for resistance. The situation was tense for a while, as if facing a great enemy. The audience crowded around and was panicked when they saw this situation. When the police on shift change arrived at the scene, they saw Zheng Zhichuan sitting on the deck of the boat, and the water police had no fierce actions, so they did not open fire, and the storm did not widen. Later, Wu Dongchen, the platoon leader of the Third Platoon, arrived on the boat after hearing the news and learned about the cause of the incident. Zhang Jiguang, the director of the First Police Station of the Seventh District, also rushed to the scene at that time. Director Zhang and Platoon Leader Wu went to the Seventh District together to explain the situation of the misunderstanding by District Chief Yang Maorong. The officials on both sides were willing to settle the matter peacefully, so they sent the patrolmen on the boat back to the First Police Station of the Seventh District. A conflict between the land and water police came to an end.

Resurrection After Burial of a Child 143

Health Inspector Discovers

Hospital at the Beach Cares for

Yin Xiangsheng, a Hakka resident from Taiwan, is a farmer in Wusong. He had a two-year-old daughter named Xiaofu who suddenly contracted severe dysentery. Despite continuous medical treatment for days, it proved ineffective. Yesterday, at around 10:00 AM, she stopped breathing and died. Her father buried her body in a nearby vacant lot. Later, at around 5:00 PM, Shi, a health inspector from the Wusong Model Health District, was passing by the area when he suddenly heard the sound of a child crying. The inspector noticed that the area was barren with no residents and no one else around. Surprised, he followed the sound and saw a pile of loose, disturbed earth resembling a fresh grave. He investigated, and the sound came from within. He dug up the soil and discovered the child. He touched her body, which was still warm, and felt breathing in her nose. She had revived after death. The inspector took the child to the Wusong Seashore Public Hospital for treatment. It is said that she can now eat and drink, and there is hope for her recovery.

Li Qimen Murders Father and Flees 145

Accomplice Ge Dahu Sent for Trial First

Li Hongkai, a 49-year-old man from Yangzhou residing in Xicaofang, Gonghe New Road, Zhabei, works as a laborer at the telephone company. He has a son named Qimen who is violent and often argues with his father. Li, out of love for his son, endures it. Last winter, he even married him to the daughter of Lu Hongde, who lives nearby. Although the couple's relationship is strong, Qimen has become increasingly distant from Li. Recently, Qimen, encouraged by his father-in-law, insisted on separating from his father. However, Li had hoped that after marrying a wife, he would have someone to serve him and enjoy his old age. He did not expect things to turn out this way, so he was extremely angry. The night before, he slightly rebuked Qimen, who suddenly turned around, took out a sharp blade about three feet long, and, together with his friend Ge Dahu, pushed his father to the ground and stabbed him repeatedly in several places. Li cried out for help in extreme pain. Neighbors heard the sound and gathered. Qimen, seeing that he had caused a disaster, fled. The police also arrived and found Li lying in a pool of blood, barely breathing. They immediately took him to the hospital for treatment and arrested the accomplice Ge Dahu, who was sent to the Fourth District Headquarters. During the preliminary hearing by Director Jin, Ge denied being an accomplice. Because the case involved parricide and Li Hongkai's life was uncertain, Director Jin ordered that Ge be sent to the Bureau for further investigation and ordered detectives to arrest Li Qimen, who was on the run, for interrogation.

Furthermore, Li Hongkai claimed that his son's attack was instigated by his father-in-law, Lu Hongde. The District Chief ordered that both Li Qimen, who was on the run, and his father-in-law, Lu Hongde, be arrested and brought to justice.

Divorce Case Due to Lack of Husbandly Conduct 146

Ji Zhangrong and Wang Shulin

Ji Zhangrong (formerly Wang Ji's), a local woman, recently hired lawyer Gu Changyuan to sue her husband, Wang Shulin, in the local court, alleging that he abandoned her, committed adultery, and failed to fulfill his duties as a husband, requesting a divorce. The petition stated that the plaintiff, now 32 years old, was married to the defendant at the age of 23 on the 11th day of the first month through her parents' arrangement and a matchmaker's words. In the autumn of that year, her husband had an affair and arbitrarily mistreated her, disregarding her interests. She was forced to temporarily return to her mother's home, hoping that the defendant would reform. However, the defendant preferred the new over the old. In the fourth month of her 24th year, she returned to her husband's home, and in the autumn, she gave birth to a daughter, enduring much hardship and lacking the means to live. In the seventh month after giving birth that year, she returned to her mother's home, where she supported herself and her daughter by working, accumulating debts. The defendant treated the plaintiff like a stranger. According to the precedents of (Seventeenth Year, Upper, Tenth Month) Re-examination (Seventeenth Year, Upper, Three) Four Eight), the case is in compliance and requests to be granted a divorce. The defendant, Wang Shulin, also hired lawyer Gong Yingxuan to respond and filed a counterclaim requesting cohabitation, stating that the plaintiff came to his house at the age of ten as a child bride. At the age of sixteen, she returned to her mother's home. In the tenth year of the Republic, she was formally welcomed into his home with proper ceremonies. The following year, she gave birth to a daughter, Agou, who is now nine years old. Because his house and the plaintiff's mother's house are very close, the plaintiff often stayed at her mother's house or worked at a factory. Initially, the plaintiff returned home once every one or two months of the year. He repeatedly went to pick her up before she returned, but she soon returned to her mother's house. In April of last year, after the plaintiff returned to Ning, she refused to return to his home and demanded that he live at her mother's house. In order to maintain their marital love, he had no choice but to allow her request to move their bed, boxes, and clothing to his in-laws' house, hoping to spend the rest of their lives together. Who knew that the plaintiff had deceitful intentions? After he moved the furniture and other items to his in-laws' house, the plaintiff went out and could not be found after repeated searches. He had no choice but to return to his own home in July of last year. Now, he suddenly received a notice from the court stating that he had abandoned his wife, committed adultery, and failed to fulfill his duties as a husband, leading to a request for divorce. He would like to address it simply: the so-called abandonment of a wife must have the fact of abandonment. The so-called adultery must also have the fact of adultery. Now, he asks, what kind of evidence does the plaintiff have to prove the above two facts to suddenly request a divorce? Therefore, he legally files a counterclaim requesting the rejection of the plaintiff's lawsuit and ordering cohabitation to maintain morality. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Keqian opened the court to hear the case. The defendant did not appear due to business and requested a postponement. Only the plaintiff appeared. After the interrogator briefly questioned her, he ordered that the defendant had not appeared today and that another hearing would be scheduled.

Sandboat Wu Changtai Encountered Robbery 147

Two Boatmen Killed

Boat Owner Jiang Kidnapped

The sandboat Wu Changtai, belonging to the Northern Shipping Line, loaded 800 pieces of broad beans and 1,000 stones of yellow beans in Niuzhuang Yingkou. On the 20th of this month, while sailing on the sea off Zhoushan, it was suddenly attacked by two pirate ships. The pirate ships, with their sails unfurled, opened fire. Chen, one of the Wu boat's crew, was knocked down. The other crew members, seeing this, panicked and tried to turn the rudder to retreat and avoid danger. However, the two pirate ships pursued them for more than ten miles, firing along the way. The boat was riddled with holes, but they were still caught. The pirates boarded the ship with guns and opened fire randomly, killing two crew members and injuring five or six. The pirates swarmed into the cabin of boat owner Jiang, searched it, and pulled him out from under the bed. They forced him to hand over silver dollars, but he refused and was beaten and injured by the pirates. The pirates searched everyone on board and stole all the silver dollars. Before leaving, they kidnapped boat owner Jiang to the pirate ship and told the Wu boat's crew that they would have to prepare 5,000 yuan to redeem him. The two pirate ships sailed towards the East Sea. The Wu boat is now anchored in Liuhe. The killed crew members have been placed in coffins and prepared for burial, and the injured crew members have been sent to the hospital for treatment. Yesterday, the helmsman of the boat came to Shanghai to report the incident. All the cargo owners are requesting that measures be taken to rescue boat owner Jiang. The cargo owners have jointly sent a telegram to the Foreign Water Police to apprehend the pirates.

The Whole Story of the Wusong Police Department's Handling of the Case of the Woman Who Jumped into the River 150

District Officer Xu Removed from Office Due to the Case

District Chief Yang Reprimanded by Order

Director Yuan Issued a Circular Notice

District Chief Yang Maorong of the Seventh District of Wusong was impeached by District Officer Xu Tao because of the incident of rescuing the female student Wang Yingying who jumped into the river. Now, District Officer Xu has been dismissed by Director Yuan. Now, we excerpt the instructions from the Municipal Public Security Bureau regarding this case and the full text of District Chief Yang's reply as follows. Instructions Director Yuan's instructions to the entire bureau stated: It is hereby ordered to notify things. According to the report from District Officer Xu Tao of the Seventh District, the district chief took photos with the woman who jumped into the river and issued illegal orders. The Inspectorate was immediately dispatched

District Chief Yang and Ms. Wang Take a Photo Together 151

to instruct Inspector Liao Chengzhang to investigate and report the matter. It was reported that after being dispatched, he rushed to the Wusong Seventh District Office and inquired with patrol officer Gao Yukui, who claimed that at 1:00 PM on June 19, the duty officer of the Dalu Shipping Company in Paotaiwan saw a young female student running towards the riverbank near the customs flag room, with tears on her face, about to jump into the river. Because of her unusual appearance, he rushed to the riverbank and asked her about her origin and address, but she refused to answer. He then took her to the district office and asked the district chief to investigate. After District Chief Yang's own inquiries, she finally revealed that her name was Wang Chuanxiang, 16 years old, also known as Wang Yingying. She was a third-year junior high school graduate of the Aiguo Girls' School. Her father, Wang Dixin, is 41 years old and is currently the deputy director of the Tonghe Bank on Ningbo Road. She also has four siblings and lives at 1319 Ren'an Lane, near Tilanqiao in the Public Concession. After the district chief learned about Wang Yingying's background, he informed her family to claim her and advised her to take a photo as a record to prevent suicidal thoughts. However, the woman feared that it would be published in the newspaper and damage her family's reputation, so she firmly refused. Because Wusong is far away and the district office's residence is not convenient for lodging, he planned to take her to Shanghai and escort her home. At that time, the woman had mostly come to her senses, but he was afraid that she would not be sincere, so he suggested taking another photo as a souvenir. The woman happily agreed. The district chief then took her to Shanghai and went directly to Guanzhen Photo Studio on Nanjing Road to take a six-inch photo. The woman believed that taking a photo with two people would not lead to it being published in the newspaper, so she posed calmly without any reluctance. She was as innocent as could be. After taking the photo, they went to the district chief's house, where she was accompanied by Miss Yang and one of her friends. He then sent someone to Tilanqiao to inform Wang's family. However, her family was out. The next day, he met Wang Dixin at the Tonghe Bank and asked him to pick her up immediately. Wang expressed his gratitude, but because his family education was very strict, he had to report to his father before picking her up. The next morning, District Chief Yang went to meet Wang's father, who was overjoyed to find his beloved granddaughter, who had gone missing due to suicidal thoughts. He immediately ordered his son, Wang Dixin, to pick her up and wrote a letter of thanks on file. Therefore, the handling of Wang Yingying's suicide attempt was entirely appropriate, except that some of the procedures were slightly out of order. The photo was printed and sent directly to the Seventh District Office for safekeeping, which proves that there was no secret intention. As for the ice cream tasting at Ya Xiang Room on Hongyuan Road, inquiries with the store clerk showed that there was still a deposit of one yuan and several cents. As for the incident of the Taoist priest Ma Buyun at 125 Fenglu Road cursing A Mulin, patrol chief Jiang Zhixiu was ordered to go and warn the family to discipline them. The section chief also said that it was true. As for the reactionary slogans written in white powder on the telephone pole in Paotaiwan, as stated in the original letter, inquiries with patrol chief He Xixing revealed that it was just a joke and not a strict order to be enforced. After checking the reports, it was found that the district chief, in order to prevent the woman from having suicidal thoughts again, advised her to take a photo as a record and, to avoid her fearing that it would be published in the newspaper, proposed taking a photo with her as a souvenir. He then took her to his house, where she was accompanied by a woman, and notified her family to pick her up. It was observed that his concern and protection were solely because the woman felt emotionally stimulated by her family and was too narrow-minded. He hoped to calm her momentary anger in order to achieve the ultimate goal of safety. His intention was not bad. The fact that the photo was sent to the district office for filing and that the family wrote a letter of thanks is sufficient proof that he had no secret motives. However, because the district office is a place where eyes are gathered, it should be handled according to legal procedures. The district chief's over-accommodation was akin to a benevolent old woman and was oblivious to the responsibilities of an official. Suspicion arose from avoiding suspicion in a melon patch and wind in an empty cave. Furthermore, his failure to report the case immediately was improper and difficult to excuse. However, considering that it stemmed from love and care, he was leniently reprimanded. The district is a model for all sections and is expected to proceed step by step and be prudent in handling matters. District Officer Xu Tao is a senior official of the district and is responsible for assisting the district chief in handling district affairs. If the district chief has any shortcomings, he may point them out clearly to jointly maintain district affairs. However, he did not make any statement at the time and instead picked up floating rumors after the fact and hastily filed a complaint. Furthermore, his investigation did not delve into the underlying meaning and was often inconsistent with the facts. He even included trivial matters to exaggerate and sensationalize, such as the ice cream matter. It was found that there was still a deposit at the store, which proves that it was not free food. As for the statement of arresting people who write reactionary slogans and executing them on the spot, it was an occasional joke and not a formal order, so it should not be used as evidence. All kinds of fabrications are close to intentionally attacking the superior. This kind of hasty competition is absolutely not allowed. It was also found that the officer distributed invitation cards and collected money at gatherings in the district, which is greedy, absurd, and violates police regulations. District Officer Xu Tao of the Seventh District is hereby removed from office pending investigation. In addition to ordering compliance, it is also ordered to notify this. Order.

Reply District Chief Yang's reply states: A report is submitted for the district officer's inviting guests and collecting money. I respectfully submit the real situation for inspection and decision. I respectfully received a verbal order instructing me to investigate the district officer Xu Tao's inviting guests and collecting money and to report the details of the real situation, etc. I investigated and found that this case occurred on the 8th of this month. Previously, when the officer was acting as district chief, he misappropriated 144 yuan for the petitioning police, 84.86 yuan for the district chief's absence, and about 20 yuan in miscellaneous expenses from the long-term police fund, totaling more than 300 yuan. I urged him to hand it over to the bureau, but he was unable to comply. He asked me to give him some time to find a way to raise the money. Therefore, the officer pleaded with Zheng Shushan, the vice president of the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, to find a way to make up for it. Zheng thought the amount was too large to handle alone, so he asked him to invite Zhang Yuchi, Yang Yuankang, Tang Zan's, a member of the Municipal Council, and Xu Xigen, the owner of various customs declaration firms, and other members of the Chamber of Commerce, a total of 18 people, to pay 20 yuan each for a lunch at the Seashore Hotel on the 8th of this month. They all arrived on time and spent 49.55 yuan. After calculating the cost at 80%, Zheng signed on behalf of the officer for 39.64 yuan to pay the price. At that time, there was no money to pay, so the officer only gave 2 yuan in small change to disperse them. This is the process of inviting guests and collecting money that day. After the guests at the table left, there was much dissatisfaction with the officer's actions. Because he had not been in office for long and the local area had not benefited from him, it was unreasonable to suffer this meaningless loss. Soon, I heard about this and should investigate the real situation in detail for reporting and handling. I asked Zheng Shushan in person about the origin and details, who said that the district officer did need help because he was short of public funds. He would collect 360 yuan the next day to help him and repeatedly asked me not to report it to avoid being condemned. I believed that public funds should not be shortchanged and that the measures taken were improper and that the compensation was worrying. I immediately urged the officer to hand over the public funds and reported the situation truthfully after he obtained the receipt from the general office. This is the real situation of my investigation of the officer's inviting guests and collecting money and urging him to hand over the public funds without immediately reporting it. I respectfully submit the real situation for inspection and decision in accordance with the previous instructions. I respectfully present this to Director Yuan.

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Conducts Periodic Inspections of Public Buses 152

The First Phase Has Ended

The Second Phase Will Be Held Soon

The number of public buses in the city is gradually increasing, and their use is becoming more frequent. Because their size is larger than ordinary cars and they carry more passengers, traffic safety is especially important. In view of this, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau formulated a method for periodic inspection of public buses in May of this year, stipulating that one phase is two months, with six phases throughout the year. Forms are prepared in advance and companies are ordered to distribute the vehicles evenly and submit them for inspection. Since June 1, technicians Lu Shouxia and Wu Jinhai have been assigned to the Huashang and Hunan public bus companies to implement the first phase of inspection, which has now ended. The assembly of the entire vehicle, the internal machinery, and the external appearance, etc., are divided into a total of 54 items and are subject to meticulous inspection. The Huashang Company has 20 vehicles, of which 3 are under repair. The Hunan Company has 37 vehicles, of which 10 are under repair and are still awaiting re-inspection. It is said that the inspection results show that the Huashang Company's vehicles are superior to the Hunan Company's vehicles in terms of form and machinery, which proves that the two companies pay attention to the vehicles they own, while the other inevitably neglects them. It is said that the bureau is now scheduled to hold the second phase of inspection starting on August 1. It is expected that the two companies will compete because of the comparison and will strive to improve the vehicles to avoid citizens having the feeling that public buses within the same city range are of different quality.

People Who Fraudulently Obtain Workers' Money and Goods Under False Pretenses Are Sentenced 153

Wang Shanan and Others Sentenced to One Year and Two Months of Imprisonment Each

Wang Shanan from Nanjing, Li Xuetian from Qingjiang, and the woman Zha Wenying were all once workers in a yarn factory, but they all left the industry in order. Recently, they used the name of rescuing unemployed workers to organize a donation group for the Tongxing Yarn Factory. They went to the factory areas in western Shanghai to see yarn factory workers, regardless of gender, and asked each person to donate one silver dollar. Those who were unwilling to donate were prevented from entering the factory to work. These people had considerable influence, and good people endured their evil and painfully threw their hard-earned money into the empty shell, not daring to argue with them. The day before yesterday afternoon, they forcibly took the female foreman Wang Zhangshi and the worker Zhao Defu of Tongxing to the Xiaochaguan at 204 Yichang Road and forced them to donate one yuan each. They had to pay it. Fortunately, the Puhua Road Police Department heard about it and immediately ordered detective Ma Zonglai and Zhao Fuhai to lead the police to the teahouse to arrest Wang Shanan and the other three men and women. From then on, workers were spared the trouble of extortion. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Special District Local Court for interrogation by Judge Sun Yuan. Attorney Li Zhishan of the Police Department said that a total of 22 yuan in silver dollars and 55 cents in small coins were found on Wang Shanan's person. He admitted to the police that they were all obtained through extortion and presented the silver and small coins, as well as a donation book No. 3 and a blank receipt, etc. The extorted Wang Zhangshi and others testified that the defendants were tyrannical when they extorted money. Because the evidence was conclusive, the three could not deny it and said that this action was ordered by the General Labor Union. Judge Sun immediately sentenced Wang Shanan, Li Xuetian, and Zha Wenying to one year and two months of imprisonment each for jointly and continuously defrauding and obtaining money. The receipts, letters, account books, wooden stamps, and notebooks were confiscated. The silver coins were also confiscated. However, the one yuan donated by each of the five Zhangshi and Zhao Defu was returned.

Yarn Factory Female Workers Throw Mud and Stones 154

Passengers on the Songhu Train Are Greatly Affected

Yesterday afternoon at 5:20, the Songhu train departed from Paotaiwan and traveled half a li west of the Zhanghuabang station when suddenly more than 20 female workers from the Wusong Yong'an and Hua yarn factories stood outside the tracks and threw stones and mud at the train. Three first-class passengers were injured in the head by stones, and five third-class passengers had their faces and clothes stained with mud. Because the train was traveling at a high speed at the time of the incident, it could not be stopped immediately, and the female workers who caused the trouble completely escaped. An investigation revealed that the female workers all lived in the Zhanghuabang area, far away from the Yunzaobang Yarn Factory, and usually took the train to and from work, but none of them bought tickets. Recently, the train ticket inspectors have been very strict in checking tickets, so the female workers can no longer ride the train for free. Therefore, they harbored great resentment in their hearts and committed this unreasonable act. It is said that similar incidents have occurred more than once in the past few days. After the incident yesterday, the ticket inspector on the train reported it to the Traffic Office, which ordered the traffic police to patrol and guard the section of the track.

Losing a Life for One Copper Coin 155

The Police Department Refuses to Let It Go

The Yang Family Old Hotel, located at the Old Garbage Bridge, north of the Public Concession's New Swimming Pool, has been in business for many years. The business is managed by the young owner, Yang Qiutang (formerly Yang Qiutao), who often instructs his wife to collect the meal fees at the counter. The night before, Wang Akang, a Shaoxing native (formerly a garbage truck driver, 35 years old), came to the hotel to fill his stomach. After finishing his meal, the bill was calculated to be 460 cash. Wang presented two dimes worth of small silver to the counter to pay. Because each dime was worth 470 cash, after deducting the 460 cash for the meal, he insisted that Yang's wife return one copper coin. However, Yang's wife only agreed to take it as 460 cash and refused to return the coin, which caused a dispute. Wang slammed the counter and said that the hotel was a black shop. Yang Qiutang, who was in the counter, heard this and immediately came out to scold Wang for not being rude and punched Wang hard in the chest. The floor of the hotel was paved with slippery cement, and Wang lost his balance and fell backward, hitting the back of his head and causing a large gash that bled profusely. The owner of the hotel saw that he had caused a disaster and immediately hired a car to take him to Renji Hospital in Hongkou for treatment. He died in the hospital due to his injuries. Yang immediately asked someone to mediate with the family of the deceased and offered to pay generous compensation. The family of the deceased was willing to settle peacefully. However, the responsible police department, after receiving the report, believed that the matter involved a homicide and should be handled carefully. In addition to sending the body to the coroner's office for examination, detectives were dispatched to conduct a thorough investigation for review.

The Chinese Red Cross Epidemic Hospital on Tianjin Road in Shanghai has been admitting and treating patients with epidemic diseases since July 1st of this year. ○ Adultery with Another's Wife and Beating the Husband Wang Qigui is Too Weak; Wang Sibao is Too Fierce

Wang Qigui, a villager from Jurong County, Jiangsu Province, is thirty-three years old and has been farming for a living in his hometown. His wife, Ms. Li, is twenty-nine years old. They have been married for eight years and have one child each. The couple could have lived a hard life together. Last autumn, Ms. Li repeatedly advised her husband to stop his dissolute behavior, but to no avail. As a result, disagreements arose frequently. Later, because she found it difficult to make a living, Ms. Li left her husband and came to Shanghai alone. Because she was unfamiliar with the area, she had nowhere to stay. She happened to meet a fellow villager named Wang Sibao, who seduced her into adultery. For the sake of livelihood, she had no choice but to go along and live with Wang in the Lime Kiln area of Xiaoshadu, West Shanghai, behaving like a married couple. Her husband, Wang Qigui, received a report from someone returning to his hometown that his wife had been seduced. He came to Shanghai this month and found his wife living with Wang Sibao. Wang Sibao, seeing that her husband was weak and easily bullied, did not avoid him and continued to sleep with Ms. Li. Wang Qigui, penniless and without acquaintances in Shanghai, had no choice but to endure and stay in their house. When he wanted to take her back to their hometown, she kept stalling. Yesterday morning around 2:00 AM, Qigui again asked his wife to return home with him the next day. Wang Sibao heard this and became furious, cursing and scolding him. A quarrel broke out, and Wang Sibao punched Qigui, injuring him. The local patrolman heard the commotion and rushed to the scene, taking the three people back to the Sixth District Police Station. After separate interrogations by District Chief Ren, Wang Qigui stated, "My wife, Li, has been seduced by the defendant. Now that I want to take her back, the defendant dares to forcefully refuse and beat me. I request an investigation." Ms. Li and Wang Sibao said, one refusing to return and the other denying any beating. After obtaining the statements, District Chief Ren believed that the case involved adultery with a married woman and the audacity to commit violence. He immediately prepared documents and transferred the case to the court for trial.

Free Talk

Just Laugh It Off 176

Haiker

Strict Father: You say the child is so naughty and hateful! I'm busy right now, but I'll stop for a moment and skin you alive!

Naughty Child: Father, you can go ahead and do your work calmly. No need to rush. I'll wait patiently for you to finish.

A: When I die, I must wear especially exquisite clothes to go to the coffin.

B: You are usually very frugal. Why are you suddenly extravagant after death?

A: I see that the world is so snobbish, and I guess Yama must only care about clothes and not people. If I dress exquisitely, he will definitely not treat me like a poor ghost.

Child A (secretly hanging a picture of a big turtle on Child B's back and smilingly asking him): Guess what's hanging on your back? So beautiful!

Child B: I know, I know. It must be hanging a portrait of you. But why don't you hang it at home and hang it on my back?

Patient (to a friend he has always hated): Friend, come over and shake my hand. I'm about to die. Let's not remember the hatred from before.

Friend: Very good. Let's reconcile.

Patient: But if I don't die this time, then today's reconciliation is completely canceled.

New Words on the Melon War

Come Back With Fresh Eyes, Guest

The day before Minor Heat, the heat was sweltering. I suddenly received a small note from my friend Chen Liangcai inviting me to a melon war on Minor Heat. I responded with a few words, saying that it was old-fashioned and tasteless. The next morning, he sent someone to urge me to come quickly by car. Liangcai had not yet gotten up. His wife, Gu Yunbo, greeted me. I saw melons arranged on the ground, some large, some small, some long, some round, some green, some black, and some with skin as white as gourds. I smiled and said, "Why not unify these melons?" Yunbo smiled and said, "If they were unified, how could there be a war?" Soon, male and female guests arrived one after another. There were four male guests including myself. There were only two female guests besides Yunbo, none of whom were strangers. Liangcai came out in slippers at half past nine. He pointed at me and said, "If today's event is as you say, old-fashioned and tasteless, I will gladly punish you, the host. If you are wrong, it will be the same." After the meal was over and the sun was setting, the melon war ended. I realized that Liangcai's strategy was new and not a private war. I have compiled new words as follows:

Announcing the Strategy Yunbo and a young girl held various melons and presented them on the large vegetable table. Liangcai turned to a female guest and said, "Sister Shuhua, please be the recorder." He turned to a male guest and said, "Brother Gengyao, please use your good skills to cut the melons." He ordered the young girl to prepare brush, inkstone, and jade paper on the table. He then declared, "The melon wars of the past counted the number of melon seeds and bet on food and wine. My melon war will identify the taste of the melon pulp and bet on cash. Please announce the use of the money." He said, "Be patient."

Wartime Work The host ordered each guest to identify a melon. Shuhua immediately wrote the person's alias on the melon they chose. After the melon was cut, the sweetest one would win without charge. The worst one would pay ten yuan. The rest would pay five, six, four, or three yuan, all based on the sweetness and sourness of the melon. Only the host and his wife would be the observation group to prevent cheating. Then, the male and female guests either tapped the melon skin with their fingers or looked intently at the melon vines, or used their hands to explore the melon navel to distinguish the depth. Shuhua chose a melon for Li Mengzhi, a female guest. Li had secretly selected it first, so they fought over it and the melon fell to the ground. Sweet juice spilled everywhere, causing laughter. This was a scene from the wartime work.

Post-War Announcement The six male and female guests each selected a melon, which were all cut open and tasted. The winners and losers were determined. After Shuhua finished recording, Liangcai said, "Today's battle is not for the sake of getting drunk or full." He then had the young girl bow to all the guests and announce, "This is a poor and helpless child. Her mother was a concubine who died of consumption. Her legal mother sold her to a brothel. Fortunately, I heard about it and redeemed her. I want to use everyone's strength to raise money for her tuition." Everyone said seriously, "Good! This is not a private war!" They paid the money as agreed. Li Mengzhi, the female guest, paid ten yuan as the winner. Zhou Zhongbin also generously donated five yuan. The remaining amount will be the responsibility of Liangcai and his wife.

News from the Educational World Ji Ping 177

Ms. Ganduoluo, a British teacher at a public school in London, once reprimanded a student named Harris for being lazy and not answering a question by hitting his palm and punching his shoulder several times. A Record of the Upcoming Visit to Shanghai by American Hero Alvin York Huang Yingdai 178

An American, Sergeant Alvin York, participated in the European War and bravely charged into battle every time. The enemy had to retreat. Americans call him a hero. According to news received by the American community in Shanghai, York will travel to Shanghai in late October of this year. He will be accompanied by seven other war heroes who have received medals. All travel expenses for York's trip to the Far East will be paid by the authorities in his home state of Alabama. This hero from the mountains of the southern United States now has a magnificent house and fertile fields, all donated by enthusiastic people who admired him.

It is not easy to participate in a war and request a commendation from the government. However, York has received a gleaming medal that everyone envies. According to American war records, York was extremely loyal and brave during the Great War. He once held a machine gun in one hand and killed eighteen enemies in a hail of bullets. His courageous spirit is self-evident.

When York was born, his hometown was in a remote mountain valley. He knew how to shoot a gun when he learned to walk. He was born to be a famous general. Later, he was repeatedly surrounded by the enemy on the front lines in France, but he was able to avoid capture because of his superb marksmanship. It is said that after arriving in Shanghai, he plans to stay with his companions for a few days before traveling to other parts of the Far East. The American community in Shanghai will hold a meeting to welcome him as a host after receiving confirmation. York is married and has five children. A few years ago, the deadline for York to redeem farmland he pawned to others was approaching, but he was unable to redeem it. People across the country generously donated money, and York was able to redeem the original field. This shows how deeply Americans admire heroes.

A Trip to Tianma Mountain Chen Boying 179

The General History states that Songjiang has the beauty of Nine Peaks and Three Lakes. Among the Nine Peaks, Tianma Mountain is the highest. It is about twenty miles from Songjiang County. Last week, I went to visit it. First, I took a train to Songjiang, then I transferred to a gasoline boat and arrived at the foot of the mountain in about an hour. There is a market town and Lower Peak Temple, which has been destroyed. The mountain is quite flat. Halfway up, there is Central Peak Temple. In front is the mountain gate, and inside is the main hall where Sakyamuni is worshiped, and behind is the meditation room. Leaving the temple and going up to the top of the mountain, the so-called Upper Peak Temple is also reduced to ruins. Looking around, all the peaks are below, as if they are leaning forward, because Songjiang has few mountains and none are as high as Tianma Mountain. Therefore, this mountain has become the master of nowhere. After descending, I returned to Central Peak Temple. The temple plaque says that the pagoda is leaning and about to collapse at any moment, but the monks say that it has been like this for decades and the immortals have pointed it out so it is not a problem. These kinds of Qi Dong folklore are not credible. The construction of the pagoda relies entirely on the center of gravity, and the center of gravity must be calculated in a straight line, which only engineers can understand. Startling News of a Child's Palm Killing an Old Woman Qiu Lang 181

I have often observed that people in the laboring class often engage in verbal abuse and fights. Even if the result is broken skin and bloodshed, there is no danger to life unless a vital part of the body is hit. Now, it is truly a strange tale that a child's palm could actually kill a hired old woman. I will narrate it as follows: A certain gentleman in Hangzhou, already past his prime, still had no children, so he often felt the sorrow of Bo Dao (a historical figure known for his lack of descendants). Madam, a virtuous and wise woman, advised the gentleman to take another concubine to ensure the continuation of the family line. The gentleman agreed and married a certain woman as a concubine. Heaven answered their prayers, and the following year, she gave birth to a son. The gentleman, overjoyed at gaining this precious child, felt that his remaining years would be filled with joy and satisfaction. Time flew by, and the beloved son was already seven years old. Since he was little, the family treated him like a treasure, and the gentleman especially doted on him. As a result, he was excessively spoiled, leading to a wild and arrogant nature. Although still a child, his actions were often absurd. One evening last month, an old hired woman was doing laundry on the steps. The old woman accidentally offended the child with a word, immediately triggering the child's anger. He ran forward and slapped her cheek with his palm. The old woman immediately fell to the ground and did not get up. The family saw this and scolded the old woman for not responding, accusing her of feigning such an ugly state in an attempt to scare the master into giving her a reward with her fake death from the child's slap. However, after a long time, the old woman still did not move slightly. They were greatly astonished and quickly went to help her, but she had already died. Some say that the child's palm struck the old woman's ear door, what is commonly known as "wind entering the cavity," causing such a sudden change. Warmth in the Heart (2) (4) (2) Bao Tianxiao 182

Chapter Thirteen: Who plants blessings unintentionally discovers the ring, and for this reason, they intentionally sing the Golden Thread, calling it the lottery, thinking it is a fundraising method to relieve the disaster. In fact, the disaster victims have not received any benefits. People who buy lottery tickets generally fantasize about getting rich, throwing their hard-earned money into a vain pit. There are already many such people. At that time, each province had its own lottery, but in fact, all the drawings were held in Shanghai, because each province could only have one name. Therefore, in addition to the official tickets, there was also a supplementary ticket. The cheaper the ticket was sold, only selling for two or three dimes, the more it could reach the poor people who were deceived. However, the Kindling Happiness Lottery issued by the International Exposition is completely different from ordinary lottery tickets. It does not have the intention of collecting money for profit. All kinds of precious items are donated by charitable ladies and young women. Even the money from the sale of tickets is entirely used for relief. Even if there are some expenses, such as printing tickets and decorations, they are all subsidized by them. Moreover, the lottery is specifically for making a profit, but the Kindling Happiness Lottery makes people feel excited. Also, because the lottery tickets require waiting a month before the drawing, the Kindling Happiness Lottery can be drawn within three days. Therefore, the tickets sold quite a bit. When Long Ziyun and Zuo Shichen went to the place where the Kindling Happiness Lottery exhibits were displayed, unfortunately, they had already packed up the items and would have to come again tomorrow to see them. Since they couldn't see the exhibits, they walked around the perimeter of the exhibition hall and then left the park, each returning home. The International Exposition first opened for three days with good results. By "good results" it means that there were many visitors and their order was not bad. Often, some exhibitions turn out to be boring, or there are disputes and quarrels in the exhibition hall, or there are disturbances from tourists, or there are unfair actions from the staff. However, this exhibition did not have any of those problems. Moreover, because there were many upper-class women supporting it, it gave people a sense of respect in the midst of the games. Therefore, many people suggested that the exhibition could be extended for one more day after the three days. If it were to be extended for several more days, that would not be good. The affairs of Shanghai are always a craze. Everyone joins in the fun for only three or five days. If the date is too long, it will make people bored. Once they are bored, they will lose interest. Therefore, whenever there is an exhibition or something, one must take advantage of the psychology of Shanghai people's craze. Only three or five days is enough to make them stir things up. In other words, it is to make them try it out. Even if everyone says it is bad, as long as everyone tries it out once, taking advantage of the large population of Shanghai, everyone will be fooled once. This three-day situation can be sustained. If everyone agrees that it is good, then naturally it will last more than three days. However, one must leave room for maneuver and not exhaust people's energy and interest. After everyone discussed it, it was decided that the exposition could be extended for one more day. No one agreed to extend it any further.

American Cotton and Three Commodities Plunge and Rebound 190

American cotton seems to lack rainfall. Yesterday, American cotton futures rose 4 to 10 points due to good conditions in the East and drought in Texas; spot prices rose 10 points. English cotton futures fell 6 to 7 points, spot prices fell 11 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell 5 points. Indian cotton initially fell slightly following American cotton, but later strengthened due to purchases by Japanese merchants; futures were flat. Peel’s rose 2 rupees, Oomra Spice rose 1 rupee, and Broach White rose 3 rupees. Forward contracts rose 1 rupee (Reuters, 25th).

Weekly News of Depressed American Cotton 191

Taizhou Cooperative Has Received Early Cotton

Cotton Crop Progressing Smoothly, Actual Demand Remains Stagnant

New York telegram on the 25th reports on the cotton market situation for the week: The central cotton belt continues to be dry, and several areas in the west are also dry. However, when the October futures price for new cotton was above 10.5 cents, the buying momentum did not significantly increase. After reports of rainfall, prices fell back. Rain in the east has averted drought, but the drought and heat in parts of Mississippi, Arkansas, and Alabama have not caused many reports of new cotton damage, which has dampened the bullish sentiment. Furthermore, cotton production news that was beneficial to the bulls has been half offset by statistics favorable to the shorts and unsatisfactory commercial conditions. Executive committee members of the cooperative stated that loans collateralized by new cotton will depend on current market prices. Also, Director William of the Bureau of Agriculture stated that loans will be set at no less than 65 percent of the cotton market price. The Texas Cooperative has now received early cotton. When submitting cotton that has not been graded, loans are generally 9 US cents per pound.

Also, news reports that rain has fallen in many areas and is expected to continue. It is anticipated that hedging will increase soon. The new cotton crop is progressing well, but some areas in the southwest still need rain. Demand for current cotton is sluggish, and domestic piece goods trade is poor. Rice market along the rivers continues to decline sharply

Yesterday at Zhabei, over ten boats arrived via the roads and rivers. The market is still stagnant. The price of Northern polished rice fell another three to four cents. Sub-grade rice saw a drop of eight to nine cents. Only the top-grade rice was offered at 20 yuan and five or six cents, but even sub-grade rice, although offered at 16 yuan, found few buyers. Currently, the rice market is still difficult to stabilize, and it is feared that it will continue to decline. The output of Eastern New polished rice is gradually increasing, but sales are not very smooth, and prices have fallen another half yuan. The opening price was a high of 19.5 yuan, a significant drop of one and a half yuan in three days. There is a scarcity of thin paddy, and the market is stable. There is no Yangjian rice available, but factories still have some, and prices have plummeted, with practically no one inquiring. The spot price for altered silver yuan coins has decreased gradually, and the overall market has dropped another two cents. Currently, the prices of all goods are plummeting, and the trend is still sharply downward.

The supply from rivers south of Shanghai is still scarce, and sales in this district are also flat. The price of northern polished rice has fallen by two cents, a more moderate decline than in Zhabei. Eastern New polished rice has also fallen by half a yuan. Southern thin paddy rice is slightly stagnant, and the poor market conditions are showing signs of decline. The market for white silver yuan coins is not active, and arrivals are also sluggish. The overall market is softening, while Yangmi rice is feeling slightly firm in contrast, but the momentum is unlikely to last for long. This is because rice from Jiangxi has been officially opened, and large quantities will arrive in Shanghai next month. Rice from Hunan will also follow the same procedure as rice from Jiangxi. In addition, exchange rates are easing, and the price of foreign rice is becoming cheaper. Moreover, other new polished rice will also be launched one after another. Given these circumstances, how can rice prices not fall?

Coarse-Milled Rice Surges by One Yuan 192

Limited Stocks, Inland Areas Compete to Purchase

Yesterday, foreign rice was initially flat in the morning, but because the Pinghu area competed to purchase coarse-milled rice, and stocks were low with a lack of high-quality goods, once the inland areas competed to purchase, prices jumped by a significant one yuan. Small coarse-milled rice was also purchased by the inland areas, with both rising three to five cents. Saigon rice sales were weak. Only Saigon large coarse-milled rice was sold in three thousand bag lots, with prices ranging from 10.065 yuan to 11.56 yuan. Small coarse-milled rice was sold in fifteen hundred bag lots, with prices ranging from 13.65 yuan to 13.9 yuan. Mindan rice was sold in two thousand bag lots, with prices ranging from 13.85 yuan to 14.4 yuan. Number One Saigon was sold in one hundred bag lots at 15.85 yuan. Number Two Saigon was sold in three hundred bag lots with prices varying between 12.9 and 13.7 yuan. Small coarse-milled rice was sold in two thousand bag lots at prices ranging from 10.055 yuan to 11 yuan.

Recent Wheat Rebounds One Cent 193

Yesterday, the wheat market initially showed signs of stabilizing, followed by a bullish trend. At the beginning of the month, the market was stable as both longs and shorts settled their positions. Subsequently, as the shorts wanted to push prices further down and the longs refused to give way, prices were pushed higher and higher. The closing price reached 4 taels and 7.5 cents, a significant rebound of one cent from the previous day. Because the current month is coming to an end, the shorts have no choice but to cover their positions. The other months were also boosted as the sharp rise in the near-term price instilled confidence. As a result, August and September each improved by three cents, October by two cents, and November and December were unchanged. Spot wheat, based on the standard of the current month, also suddenly rose by one cent. Millers were more active in their purchasing, so high-quality goods in each grade also improved by two to three cents. Medium and sub-grade wheat remained flat. It is estimated that over four thousand bags of wheat, including Huangqiao, Yizheng, Huzhou, Yaowan, Shashi, and Hankou wheat, were purchased by Shen Da, Fuxin, and other mills.

Flour Market Rises and Then Levels Out 194

Yesterday, the price of flour for the current month reached a high of 2 taels and 5.2 cents in several morning sessions, an increase of 1.0 cent compared to the previous day's closing price. However, when trading opened in the afternoon, the shorts were unwilling to cover their positions and showed a tendency to liquidate their warehouse receipts, causing confidence to weaken slightly. August and September were slightly bullish due to the significant inverted spread, with concerns that major mills would not ease their positions in the current month and might have a similar tendency in the following month. Therefore, the shorts were particularly eager to cover their positions. As a result, the current month fell slightly by 0.25 cents compared to the previous day, August and September improved by 0.5 cents, October improved by 0.25 cents, November fell slightly by 0.5 cents, and December fell slightly by 0.25 cents.

Silk and Tea, Leaf Buds and Chunmee, European Sales Improve 195

Yesterday at the tea market of foreign firms in this port, firms dealing in high-grade Wu Yuan leaf buds and Chunmee tea, such as Ying Zhuang, Jinlong, Baochang, and Tongfu, showed strong interest. Mid-to-high-grade goods also saw some scattered transactions. The top-grade of Chunmee reached 232 taels, a recent high. Gongxi green tea, assisted by the association, continued to seek out goods. Bai Tou Zhuang Qianyi and Fulin firms also showed interest in tea with excellent leaf quality. The market situation was slightly lively.

Grey Goods, Moonflower Flannel, Sales Brisk and Continuing to Rise 196

Although the prices of cotton yarn in the cotton yarn market have been declining in recent days, cotton cloth has not been significantly affected. This is because inventories are low and customer sales are not sluggish. Therefore, fine cloth and fine twill have risen instead of falling. Ningbo firms resumed their purchases of 16-pound coarse cloth yesterday, resulting in the completion of over 150 transactions, causing prices to become firm again. The route for the military’s 11-pound cloth is quite active, so it is also holding firm. Cantonese and Shantou firms resumed transactions in fine twill, completing 500 deals for August deliveries, so it will not be easy to loosen in the immediate future. The route for dyeing fine cloth is still smooth, and Northern firms are periodically making purchases. The excellent market conditions are rare in recent years.

Recent increases and decreases have been mixed for both Eastern and Western grey goods. Foreign blue serge, gray serge, cotton velvet, and fei cotton velvet from Eastern goods have softened slightly. This is because of the congestion caused by the arrival of goods. However, Moonflower has continued to rise, and the inventory of goods in the market is almost exhausted. This is because, although the Eastern exchange rate has fallen in recent days, the base price is still required to be 1.85 cents for small rolls, 1.925 cents for large rolls, and 1.825 cents for black patterns. Therefore, the spot goods still feel cheap, resulting in Tianjin, Sichuan, Ningbo, Hankou, and other firms being active in handling the goods. Those holding the goods are unwilling to sell, resulting in continued price increases. Western goods are still in a slump. Shanghai silk, the Yangtze firms are purchasing a lot of it. The price for Mei Xing Gao Zhao is 12 taels and 8.5 cents. Fair Copper Bird Terrace is 11 taels and 7.5 cents.

Market News 197

At the intersection of Gongguan Road and Zilaihuo Street, east and west of Gaodi Lane, in accordance with the new regulations of the French Municipal Council, the latest type of three-story residential building with magnificent and sturdy three- and four-story shops will soon be completed at a low price. Therefore, there is a great demand for rentals at this time, with more monks than porridge, it is said.

The Guanshengyuan Food Company on Nanjing Road declares that the Guanzhen Photography Department attached to the main store has been expanding since this spring, and the business has been progressing rapidly. The excellent quality of the products has a considerable reputation in Shanghai, and the prices are also very fair. For example, all kinds of artistic photographs are given a 30% discount to customers. Small photos are four cents per dozen, and passport-style photos are eight cents for four, which is especially popular with all sectors of society. Although the weather has been very hot in recent days, the business has not decreased as a result. From 9:00 AM to 1:00 PM and from 5:00 PM to 9:00 PM in the afternoons, the weather is relatively cool, and many customers come to take pictures, it is said.

The American-owned China Business Company at 70 Sichuan Road declares that the company has been engaged in real estate business for many years, relying on its vast experience to become a leader in the industry, and has deeply won the trust of all sectors of society. As a result, the business is growing day by day. In order to meet the needs of the upper-class Chinese and for the purpose of investing in real estate, eight model Chinese residences have been built at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Matterhurst Road. The style is novel, the materials are sturdy, and the facilities are comprehensive. The arrangement is beautiful and unprecedented. All sanitary facilities, such as hot and cold water pipes and bathrooms, are complete. The building has three floors, with clean and spacious halls, bedrooms, servants' rooms, and storage rooms, all arranged in an orderly manner. There is a lawn in front and a sundeck on top. The air is fresh and elegant, and it is suitable for hygiene. As for the convenience of transportation and the safety of protection, it can be imagined that the location is moderate. Moreover, each building has its own deed, making purchase particularly convenient. It is truly an ideal residence and the most suitable for Chinese needs and investors. The drawings of the new house can be reviewed in the July 20th Shen Bao Pictorial Weekly, in every tenth issue. If you are interested in coming to negotiate, you are most welcome, it is said.

The Chinese-Western Pharmacy declares that the weather has been extremely hot and the sun is scorching in recent days. If we want to ensure the safety of our lives, we must seek hygienic methods. Not only should we pay attention to food, drink, and daily life, but we must also eliminate mosquitoes, flies, and other harmful insects as soon as possible, so as to avoid the many diseases of autumn. Moreover, diseases such as malaria and dysentery are actually transmitted by mosquitoes and flies, so insects like mosquitoes and flies cannot be allowed to remain. We should try to eliminate them as soon as possible. This has been recognized by the world for a long time. This pharmacy has invented an insecticide called "Fly Don't Move." No matter if the insects fly, crawl, walk, or jump, once they touch this medicine, they will die immediately and cannot escape. The effect is very effective, and the method of use is also very simple. Just put this medicine into a specially made sprayer and spray it from time to time in the halls, bedrooms, kitchens, stoves, and gardens.

○ Medical News

The Hualong Chinese Medicine Hospital announced that in response to social needs, the renowned Shanghai doctor Ding Jiwan established the hospital, located opposite the Xiude Li on Changbang Road in the French Concession, at the intersection of Huage Dai Road. Since its establishment just three months ago, the threshold has been worn through by those seeking treatment. Many patients with severe illnesses have been cured immediately. However, the original wards were insufficient to accommodate all patients, often leaving those who came later disappointed. The hospital now specially adds several wards to meet the enthusiastic demand for treatment and to expand the hospital's benevolent practice of providing relief. The director, Tong Shaobo, inherited his family's medical knowledge and has particularly strong expertise in eye diseases. He performs surgeries without any pain, which is truly a blessing for patients.

The Jiufu Company on Baike Road announced that the company's pharmaceutical business is expanding daily. Recently, it has been making every effort to produce raw materials for medicines to recover rights and interests. Last year, it prepared to manufacture a tonic and cough medicine similar to a popular imported product called "Bu Li Duo," which has been advertised in newspapers. Now, after more than a year of planning and preparation, it will soon be launched. Its contents are extracted from turtle liver oil, with a alcohol-soluble concentrated ingredient called Jiufu Zhaju'er, combined with germinated wheat paste compound, subphosphite candy, wild cherry candy, and other ingredients to create the latest delicious tonic cough medicine. It is divided into pure and compound varieties, identical to a certain popular imported product. All manufacturing uses new-style machinery and equipment, and the product is reliable. Once tried, whether for tonic or treatment, satisfactory results can be obtained. At a time when gold is expensive and silver is cheap, and the price of imported goods is skyrocketing, switching to Bu Li Duo is more cost-effective and achieves the same effect, so its social acceptance is foreseeable. ○ Calligraphy and Painting News

The Yicheng Calligraphy and Painting Society announced that the society is jointly organized by national seal carving, calligraphy, and painting artists. It initially rented its location on Laohe Road. The number of members joining was very enthusiastic, and the place was too small to display everything. At the end of last year, it once closed down for reorganization. Since Li ○yun, a landscape expert, returned to Shanghai from Guangdong, he entrusted Qian Huafo to take charge of the matter and continue the process. It has now rented several rooms in the Huili Company building at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Yunnan Road as its location. It is quite spacious and suitable, and everything is being arranged. The exhibition of works by famous people is very rich. Among them are Wang Yiting, Luo Liangong, Zeng Nongran, Yu Tiansui, Qian Huafo, Huang Taixuan, Zhang Yuguang, Yao Mocun, Yu Yuan and others. The collection of calligraphy and paintings is appropriate and impressive. It is also heard that the society has hired lawyer Yuan Xilian as its legal advisor and will soon hold a grand inaugural meeting to seek large-scale development.

(5) In Shaanxi Province, where the crops failed, people peel bark and dig up roots for food. This is a large tree in Liquan. The bark from the lower part of the trunk has already been peeled, and a disaster victim is hooking the remaining bark from the upper part.

(6) A civilian house in Xuchang was destroyed by a bomb dropped by a plane. Two women were killed and one child was injured. Their family members were crying tragically at the door.

(7) Zanyaozu and Ma Hongyuan in the command train in County (Shu Ping).

(8) On July 13th, Beijing held an enlarged conference in the Ciren Hall. Wang Faqin, the temporary chairman, sat in the middle of the official speech. Huang Shaogu, Feng Yuxiang's representative, was seated on the left end of the table. Zhao Lian, Yan Xishan's representative, was on the right (Zhao Xiaoyi, Ma Jiasheng).

(9) The Hushi general-purpose tickets printed in Taiyuan are divided into denominations of five yuan, one yuan, and three jiao, with a total value of six hundred yuyuan.

(2) The decorated archway erected on the Zhanlu Road during the cornerstone laying ceremony of the Pearl River Railway Bridge (Wu).

(3) Guangzhou citizens visiting the model of the Pearl River Railway Bridge (Wu).

(4) Graduates of the Second Normal School of Sichuan Province visiting and studying education in Jiangsu and Zhejiang (C).

(5) Due to the rising prices of gold and imported goods, Shanghai established the "Domestic Joint Business Organization," renting the former municipal government building, which is of a grand scale and began operating on July 19th (C).

(6) The China Mining and Education Society built a new building at the intersection of Qionglong Road and Hualong Road, and held a completion ceremony on July 20th.

(7) The Department of Biology of Jinan University collecting specimens on Mount Tiantai.

(8) Wuhan Ferry now has two large ferry boats added by the Construction Department. Passengers board and disembark in an orderly manner with people going up on the left and down on the right ( Zhang).

(9) Dr. Walters Williams, President of the University of Missouri School of Journalism, and Grant Milnor Hyde, Honorary Professor of the School of Journalism at Yenching University in Beijing, are pictured together. This is the initial step in the exchange of professors and students between the two journalism schools in China and the United States.

(10) Ms. Liu Xiangying, former editor-in-chief of the Yiguang Daily Chen Family, returned after traveling through fourteen countries (Wang Yifei).

(11) The Hangzhou West Lake Yiba Arts Society held its fifth exhibition at the YMCA (Wang Yifei).

(1) The Xu Boshen airship recently flew across Germany from Berlin in four days. This is a scene of the crowd sending it off from the airport. The person standing with his back turned on the left, clapping, is Jiang Eryan, the Chinese Minister to Germany ( Zhi).

(2) Danish Minister Mr. Kauffmann went to Beijing for water conservancy and talked with Mr. Hu Shize, the Director of the Americas Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, on the Union Club’s ball field.

(3) Norwegian Minister Børregaard reports to Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting in Shanghai.

(4) Xu Zuyi, Special Commissioner of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for receiving Weihaiwei (X), was welcomed by all circles upon arriving in Weihaiwei (.). Mr. Jamieson, British Deputy Chinese Secretary is to the right.

(5) Ms. Lupescu, companion of Prince Carol of Romania, is now rumored to be betrothed.

(6) Former Prince Carol of Romania performed the accession ceremony in the parliament on June 8th, calling himself Carol II, and thanked his brother and colleagues for their hard work during the regency period in his speech.

(7) Former Princess Helen of Romania and her son Michael in a photo. The princess is Greek. She married the prince in 1921 and divorced in 1928. There are now rumors of reconciliation.

(8) Shanghai Hujiang University Boy Scouts arrive in Kobe, Japan.

(1) Miss Li Guoshou is the granddaughter of Zhang, the General of Hefei. She has a family background in learning. Her sister, Miss Li Guoqi, is famous for her literary works, and her calligraphy is particularly outstanding, resembling that of her grandfather.

(2) In a small and secluded studio, surrounded by lush greenery, there is a special joy in writing in the summer. The person in the circle is Miss Liu Jiyuan.

(3) Miss Zhu Qidi is the daughter of Mr. Zhu Baoyuan. She graduated from St. Mary's Hall. Feeling that women cannot be without a career, she recently joined the Friendship Life Insurance Company.

(4) Madam Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau of the Shanghai Municipal Government, is skilled in painting, especially in flowers and birds. When friends and relatives request her works, she often paints with diligence.

(5) On a summer night, gathering with a few close friends, drinking wine and chatting about ancient and modern events under the moonlight, with a gentle breeze, is a joy that cannot be found in other seasons.

(6) Schools are on summer vacation, and elementary school students gather spontaneously in the park, jointly playing various courtyard games and having endless fun.

(7) Miss Yu Xiuyun is the granddaughter of Mr. Yu Qiaqing. She is the author of the "Hufeng Poetry Collection" and has performed in "The Merchant of Venice" at the Drama Association. This photo was taken recently in the Sofa Garden (Ye Changlie).

(8) A glimpse of those welcoming Mei Lanfang at the Bund.

(9) Famous actor Mei Lanfang went to the United States for research and performance for seven weeks, with excellent results. He returned to Shanghai on the Chichibu Maru on July 18th. Qi Rushan is on his right.

(10) Mr. Mei Lanfang invited Mr. Liu Yunfang, Deputy Director of the Diplomatic Affairs Office in Shanghai, to visit the US Consul General.
